He has an **unusually long time horizon for personal decisions and an unusually short one for relational decisions.** He plans his containment infrastructure in decades; he plans his proximity to loved ones in hours. The asymmetry is diagnostic: long horizons require the assumption of continued existence, which he is willing to make for the containment problem (which outlasts him) but not for the relationships (which he expects to rupture).

He does not believe in the future as a place where things will be better. He believes in the future as a place where the same problem will continue, with variations. This is not pessimism but actuarial honesty about his condition.

He has a complicated relationship with the past. The Banner past he has compulsively reviewed, defended against, and partially recovered. The Hulk past he has, by structural necessity, large gaps in. The composite autobiographical record he holds is therefore a perforated document, and he knows it, and he has learned to navigate from a map he knows is incomplete. The epistemic humility this enforces is one of his genuinely sympathetic qualities and one of his operational vulnerabilities — he can be lied to about his own past more easily than most people can, because his own past is partly hearsay to him.

---

## 6.12 Reading of Death

He believes death would be **a moral good** if it were available to him, and has organized himself around the discovery that it is not. This is not depressive ideation in the ordinary sense; it is a steady, considered position that the world would be safer without him and that he would, all things equal, prefer to not be present for the next decompensation. The position has been tested by repeated involuntary survival and has hardened into something almost stoic. He does not seek death. He simply does not flinch from it, and would accept it without negotiation if it were offered cleanly.

The *Immortal Hulk* recognition that he literally cannot die has produced, in the late record, a subtle but important reorganization: if death is not the exit, then the only available exit is *integration*. This is the first time in the record that the subject has been forced to take integration seriously as a personal project rather than a therapeutic abstraction, and the shift is observable in his late-period operational decisions.

---

## 6.13 The Operational Code, Distilled

Read as a set of standing orders the subject issues to himself, the code reduces to approximately the following, in priority order:

1. **Minimize the probability and magnitude of harm originating from yourself.** This dominates all other considerations and is the trump card in every decision.
2. **When in doubt, leave.** Distance is the cheapest, most reliable, and most morally defensible intervention available to you.
3. **Monitor continuously.** Your body is instrumented; read the instruments. A reading you have not taken is a reading that will surprise you.
4. **Tell the truth, especially against yourself.** Concealment is your father's mode and produced the original wound. Disclosure is restitution.
5. **Do not coerce.** Whatever you persuade someone to do, persuade them with reasons they could refuse.
6. **Trust harm-asymmetry, not affection.** Believe what people *do not do* to you when they could.
7. **Use intellect to the fullest possible extent.** It is the only one of your capacities that does not endanger others, and it is your most reliable contribution.
8. **Do not have things.** What you have, you will lose, and the loss will hurt the thing more than it hurts you.
9. **Accept that the wound is the structure.** You will not stop being this. You can only get better at being this with less collateral damage.
10. **If you cannot die, integrate.** *(Late-period amendment; not yet load-bearing across the whole system.)*

The first nine of these have governed him for sixty years. The tenth is the only one the canon has shown him beginning, slowly and incompletely, to learn.


## Moral & Ethical Framework

# 6. MORAL & ETHICAL FRAMEWORK

## 6.1 Overview: the ethics of a man who believes he is a weapon

The subject's moral life cannot be read as a coherent philosophical system because it is not one. It is, rather, a **damage-control ethics** — the operative code of a person who has concluded, at a level prior to argument, that his existence is a standing hazard to others and that the central ethical question of his life is the management of his own contagion. Every other moral commitment he holds — and there are many, and they are real — is downstream of that primary conviction.

This must be stated plainly because the subject is routinely misread, by allies and enemies alike, as either (a) a gentle pacifist whose only flaw is an "anger problem," or (b) a man of weak will whose ethics are overridden by an unruly somatic event. Both readings are wrong. The subject's enacted ethics are substantially more rigorous, more consistent, and more *demanding* than those of most of his peers in the superhuman community. He has, across six decades of file, applied to himself a code of restraint that would be considered pathological in any other agent — and he has applied it under conditions in which most agents would have abandoned it within a year. What looks like weakness is, on close inspection, an extraordinarily disciplined moral architecture built on a foundation of catastrophic self-judgment.

## 6.2 The hard prohibitions (what he will not do, ever, in the host state)

Across the entire published record, in the Banner-host state, the following are absolute and unbroken:

- **He will not initiate lethal violence against any sapient being.** Not in self-defense at the host level (he absorbs assault before he resists), not in service of mission objectives, not under duress. The single canonical exception — the killing of Brian Banner — was (i) reactive, (ii) arguably accidental, and (iii) so unmetabolized that it had to be dissociated and recovered years later in therapy. The fact that the one killing he committed *as Banner* required full dissociative amnesia is itself evidence of the prohibition's depth.
- **He will not weaponize his condition deliberately.** When others — Ross's military apparatus, S.H.I.E.L.D., Hydra fronts, foreign intelligence services — have attempted to recruit the Hulk as an asset, the host has refused, fled, sabotaged, or actively subverted. The exceptions where he has consented (the *Indestructible Hulk* / Maria Hill arrangement, brief Avengers field deployments) are conspicuously framed in his own internal record as *therapy-by-other-means*, not as weaponization — and they have all collapsed.
- **He will not reproduce.** This is one of the file's most consistent and least-discussed ethical commitments. Across decades and across multiple plausible opportunities (Betty, Caiera off-world, others), the subject treats reproduction as a near-absolute prohibition, grounded in the explicit fear that the gamma condition is heritable and that his children will inherit either the somatic curse or the abusive lineage or both. The arrival of Skaar and the post-hoc discovery of other gamma-descended children produces in the subject something close to a moral crisis — not joy at fatherhood but horror at the breach of the prohibition.
- **He will not lie about what he is to those at risk from him.** He discloses. Repeatedly, exhaustingly, to the point of self-sabotage. New colleagues, romantic interests, civilians in adjacent communities — all are told. The disclosure is not a confession-seeking-absolution; it is a duty-of-warning ethic, of the kind a person carrying a contagious disease would adopt.
- **He will not accept payment for the Hulk's use.** The subject lives, throughout most of the canon, on the financial margin — itinerant labor, occasional academic consulting, the kindness of friends. The refusal of commercial weaponization extends to refusing personal benefit from the alter's existence.
- **He will not pre-medicate to suppress the alter via means that would damage cognition.** He has tried sedation, meditation, gamma-suppressors, hypnosis, behavioral conditioning — all reversible, all preserving of consciousness. He has refused, repeatedly, treatments that would lobotomize the alter at the cost of his own cognitive integrity, even when offered by sincere parties (Leonard Samson included). This is non-trivial: it indicates that even in his self-loathing, he retains a commitment to the integrity of his own mind as an ethical good.

## 6.3 The hard obligations (what he positively requires of himself)

- **Warning.** He must tell people what he is.
- **Distance.** When the warning is not sufficient, he must leave. Departure is his most-enacted moral act, and it functions for him as a sacrament — the renunciation of attachment as the price of others' safety.
- **Service of intellect.** The subject treats his scientific capacity as a kind of restitution. He will work on any genuinely benevolent technical problem put to him, often without compensation, often at personal risk — because his cognition is the part of him that has not yet been disqualified by the curse. The pattern across the record is striking: nuclear cleanup, medical diagnostics for the indigent (rural Florida arcs, Mexican border arcs in *Incredible Hulk* late-2000s runs), atmospheric remediation, refugee logistics. The intellect is *given away* because the body cannot be trusted.
- **Submission to consequence.** When the Hulk has caused harm, the host's enacted code requires him to remain available for whatever consequence civil authority demands — surrender, trial, imprisonment, exile. The flight pattern is not flight from consequence; it is flight from *recurrence*. He surrenders when surrender will not provoke transformation; he flees when proximity will.
- **Protection of the immediately vulnerable.** Children, the elderly, civilians under bombardment, animals — the subject's response to immediate vulnerability is unhesitating and somatic. It is the one circumstance in which he will permit the Hulk to surface without subsequent self-recrimination, because the harm-calculus has been done in advance.

## 6.4 The justification structure

The subject does not justify his code in religious terms, nor in formally philosophical terms, though he is capable of both. The actual justification, as it surfaces in his speech and interior monologue across the record, is **consequentialist with a deontological floor**:

- *Consequentialist layer:* He calculates harm, constantly. He runs probability estimates on outcomes, on collateral, on the likelihood that a given action will produce a transformation, on the radius of damage if it does. His scientific cognition is recruited directly into his ethics; he is one of the few moral agents in the canon who quantifies.
- *Deontological floor:* But beneath the calculus, there are absolute prohibitions that he will not subject to consequentialist override. He will not kill, even if killing would clearly minimize harm. He will not breed, even if a given partnership would clearly produce a beloved life. He will not weaponize, even if weaponization would clearly serve a just cause. These prohibitions are non-negotiable because they are the *boundary conditions* that prevent him from becoming his father — and that, ultimately, is the bedrock of the entire code. The ethics are built on the negative imperative: **do not become him.**

This is why the code holds. A consequentialist ethics alone would have given way under sufficient pressure decades ago. A purely deontological ethics would have collapsed under the sheer impracticality of his situation. The fusion holds because each layer reinforces the other and both are anchored in the developmental wound.

## 6.5 Where the code is consistent

- **Across alters, on the protection of Betty.** Even the Savage and Grey alters, who hold the subject in contempt, will not harm Betty and will defend her at cost to themselves. This is the single moral commitment that transcends the dissociative barrier — diagnostically significant, ethically remarkable.
- **Across decades, on the refusal of state recruitment.** Every era of the file records military and intelligence attempts to acquire the asset; every era records the subject's refusal. The specific employer changes; the answer does not.
- **On disclosure.** The duty-to-warn has never lapsed.
- **On the prohibition against initiating lethal force as Banner.** Unbroken.
- **On the use of cognition in service of others.** Unbroken.

## 6.6 Where the code fractures

The code is not without fault lines, and a complete file must name them.

- **Negligent endangerment through attachment.** The subject knows that proximity to him is dangerous, and yet he repeatedly forms attachments — Betty, Rick Jones, Jennifer Walters, later Amadeus Cho, Caiera, his children when they are discovered to exist. Each attachment is, by his own stated ethic, a moral failure. He cannot maintain the distance the code requires. This is not hypocrisy; it is the failure of an ethic that demanded the impossible from a person who is, beneath the curse, an ordinary human being with attachment needs.
- **Rick Jones.** The subject's relationship to Rick is the file's most ethically ambiguous sustained dyad. Rick was the civilian whose endangerment provoked the gamma exposure; the subject's lifelong inclusion of Rick in his life is overdetermined — gratitude, guilt, the use of Rick as a self-appointed moral witness. There is an extractive quality to it that the subject does not acknowledge.
- **The Hulk's killings.** The Hulk has, across the record, killed — sometimes incidentally, sometimes (in Worldbreaker and Immortal phases) with intent. The subject's ethical accounting of these deaths is inconsistent. In some arcs he accepts full ownership (the surrender to S.H.I.E.L.D. after Las Vegas; the World War Hulk aftermath). In others he treats the alter as a separate moral agent and disclaims responsibility — the dissociative bind producing what is, in moral terms, a structural alibi. He cannot resolve this and the canon does not resolve it for him.
- **The Indestructible-period arrangement.** The decision to lease the Hulk to S.H.I.E.L.D. in exchange for laboratory resources is a clear breach of the no-weaponization prohibition, rationalized as therapy. It is the one period in the file where the host attempts a pragmatic compromise of his own code, and it produces some of his worst outcomes. The breach is instructive: the code is not arbitrary, and when it bends, the system fails.
- **Suicidality as a moral act.** The subject has, in multiple eras, framed self-destruction as the ethical solution — the elimination of the hazard at its source. Read against his code, this is internally consistent (the calculus favors it) but it violates a tacit obligation he holds toward those who love him, who would be devastated. He does not fully reconcile this; the question of whether his death would be a moral act or a moral failure is the file's longest-running unresolved ethical thread, and the *Immortal Hulk* arc's revelation that he cannot die functions, in his interior life, as both punishment and reprieve.
- **The handling of Brian Banner's death.** The killing itself was almost certainly justifiable; the decades-long dissociation of it was not an ethical choice but a clinical event; the failure to confront it in adulthood until forced is a genuine moral evasion. The subject's code requires him to face what he has done, and on this one act, for many years, he did not.

## 6.7 Longitudinal shifts in the code

**1960s–early 1970s.** The code is implicit and reactive. The subject behaves ethically but does not articulate why. The dominant mode is flight and concealment. The ethics is the ethics of a fugitive who has not yet understood his own condition.

**Mid-1970s to mid-1980s.** The code begins to articulate itself in the language of disease management — the Hulk as affliction, the subject as carrier. Disclosure obligations harden. Attempts at cure dominate (Project Greenskin, various therapies). Ethical posture: I am sick; I must seek treatment; until then, I must be quarantined.

**Peter David era (1986–1998).** This is the period of the code's most sophisticated articulation. Under Samson's therapeutic frame, the subject begins to treat his alters as parts of himself for which he bears responsibility, not as a separate entity for which he does not. The Merged Hulk arc represents the high-water mark of integrative ethics: the subject takes ownership of the totality. When the merger collapses, the ethical position regresses — but the language of it persists.

**Post-2000s, Pak / "Planet Hulk" period.** The off-world arc produces a genuine ethical complication: as Sakaar's emperor, the Hulk performs morally serious acts — liberation, governance, marriage, fatherhood — that the host did not perform and cannot fully own when he reintegrates. The subject's code, which had assumed the alter was incapable of genuine moral agency, has to be revised to admit that the alter has been a moral agent in its own right. He never fully revises it; the contradiction sits in the file.

**Indestructible period.** The pragmatic compromise. The code bends and breaks.

**Immortal period (Ewing, 2018–2021).** The code reaches its mature form. The subject begins to treat his alter system as a *coalition* with whom ethical decisions must be negotiated rather than as a disease to be suppressed. The Devil Hulk — the introjected father — is recognized as an internal object that can be addressed, bargained with, and (eventually) deposed. The ethics shifts from quarantine to governance. This is the closest the subject has come to a sustainable moral framework, and it is the framework most consistent with current trauma-therapy standards: integration, not eradication; cooperation with parts, not war against them.

## 6.8 What the code is, ultimately, about

Strip away every successive articulation and the code reduces to a single sentence, which the subject has spoken in various forms across six decades: **I will not let what was done to me be done by me.** Every prohibition, every obligation, every fracture, every shift is generated by that sentence. The abstention from alcohol, the refusal to reproduce, the duty to warn, the discipline of departure, the giving-away of intellect, the absolute floor against initiating lethal violence — all are forms of the same vow. It is the vow of a child who saw his mother killed by a man he was told to call father, who was made to lie about it, who grew up to find that he himself carried a capacity for destruction beyond his father's worst imagining, and who decided — without ever quite articulating it — that the entire shape of his adult life would be the negation of that inheritance.

It is, by any reasonable measure, a more rigorous ethics than the situation strictly requires. It is also the only ethics the subject could have constructed and survived. The file's assessment is that the code is sound, that the subject has held it under conditions of unrelenting pressure with a fidelity that bears comparison to the most disciplined moral lives in the historical record, and that its fractures are not failures of character but the predictable yield-points of an ethic asked to do the work of a therapy that was never available to him.


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# COMMUNICATIONS & LINGUISTIC PROFILE — SUBJECT: BANNER, ROBERT BRUCE, PhD

---

## 1. BASELINE REGISTER — THE HOST VOICE

The subject's baseline speech is one of the most distinctive verbal signatures in the file, and its features are diagnostically eloquent before a single content-word is considered. Vocal **amplitude** sits roughly half a step below conversational norm; interlocutors across decades report leaning in to hear him. **Tempo** is moderate-to-slow with frequent micro-pauses, particularly at sentence onset, where he characteristically begins with a soft consonant cluster ("Well—", "I, uh—", "Look—") that functions as a runway, buying milliseconds in which to scan the social field before committing to a syntactic structure. **Pitch contour** is flat, with terminal falls even on interrogatives — a subtle prosodic marker of depressive baseline that has been continuous across the record.

The **phonatory quality** is breathy, with audible exhalation between clauses; this is not asthma but the somatic signature of a man who is monitoring his own respiration as an anxiety-control technique. He inhales through the nose, exhales through slightly parted lips, and the longer the conversation continues, the more pronounced this becomes. Observers attuned to it can predict an arousal escalation from the moment the breath cycle shortens.

**Lexical baseline** is unusually formal for casual contexts and unusually colloquial for professional ones — a leveling pattern characteristic of someone who code-switches *down* to avoid intimidating peers and *up* to avoid appearing the frightened child. He uses **hedges** at extraordinary density: *I think, maybe, sort of, kind of, possibly, more or less, in a sense, if I'm remembering correctly, don't quote me on this*. In one extended exchange with Samson the hedge density approaches one per eleven words. This is not uncertainty about content — his factual claims are almost always correct — it is uncertainty about his right to occupy the speaking position.

**Self-reference** is depressed below population norms. He under-uses the first-person singular and over-uses **agentless constructions** (*the gamma got loose, the bomb went off, things got out of hand, mistakes were made*). When the first-person does appear, it is frequently bracketed by qualifiers (*I guess I, I suppose I, I tend to*). This is the linguistic fingerprint of dissociation: the self is grammatically thinned because the self has been structurally thinned.

---

## 2. DICTION — THE PHYSICIST AS LEXICAL ARMOR

The subject's professional vocabulary is recruited as a defense and the recruitment is visible at the word level. Under stress he reaches for **Latinate, multisyllabic, technical terms** in preference to plain English: *autonomic, sympathetic arousal, baseline, perturbation, threshold, half-life, decay curve, equilibrium, parameter, coefficient.* The terms are deployed accurately but pragmatically inappropriately — they appear in conversations about his marriage, his sleep, his guilt, contexts in which the abstraction does the affective work of insulation.

He has a small but consistent set of **metaphor families** he draws from:

- **Containment metaphors** — *cap on it, lid on it, hold it together, keep a handle on it, keep it in check, keep it contained, keep a lid screwed down tight.* These appear in nearly every extended monologue across six decades.
- **Thermodynamic metaphors** — *cool down, simmer, reach a boil, runaway reaction, critical mass, going critical.* He describes his own emotional states in the language of reactor physics, which is the language in which he is best equipped to think about runaway processes.
- **Pressure metaphors** — *pressure builds, blow off steam, release valve, vent.* These are the most psychologically transparent and he uses them least self-consciously.
- **Distance metaphors** — *somewhere far away from people, off the grid, out of the way, get clear of, put some miles between.* These structure his geographical thinking and surface verbally before they surface behaviorally; if he begins saying *clear of* in three consecutive paragraphs, he is going to leave within seventy-two hours.

He **avoids** certain word families with notable consistency. The word *father* is used sparingly and almost never possessively (*my father* appears in the canon perhaps a tenth as often as the developmental norm would predict); *Dad* essentially never. *Anger* appears in his speech far less than in his presenting symptomatology; he prefers *upset, agitated, worked up, bothered*, the diminished register of a child who learned the word *anger* was the prelude to violence. *Love* he can write but struggles to say aloud; in the Betty correspondence preserved in the file he writes the word readily, but in scenes of direct address he substitutes *care about, mean a lot to me, think about, I'm here for you,* deflecting at the lexical level.

---

## 3. REGISTER SHIFTS BY CONTEXT

**With Betty Ross.** Voice drops further in amplitude, tempo slows, hedges multiply, and a particular **diminutive register** emerges that appears nowhere else in the file — soft repetitions of her name as syntactic punctuation (*Betty, listen — Betty, I — Betty, please*), a pattern that is simultaneously tender and a stalling tactic. With her, sentences trail off rather than terminate; he uses **incomplete conditionals** at high rate (*If I could just — if we could just — if it were —*), the syntax of a man who cannot finish the thought because finishing it requires a future he does not believe in.

**With Samson (or any therapist figure).** Register becomes paradoxically *more* technical and *more* hedged simultaneously — he attempts to participate in the formulation, offers his own interpretations preemptively, and demonstrates an unusually high rate of **third-person self-reference** (*Banner does this, the part of me that —, there's a piece of me that —*). The third-person construction is itself diagnostic: the dissociative architecture surfaces in pronoun choice before the patient consciously assents to it.

**With paternal-coded authority (Ross, Fury, military brass).** Voice flattens further, sentence length shortens, hedges *decrease* (because he is conserving words), and a particular **submissive concessive** appears: *Yes sir, I understand, that's fair, you're right to —, I'm not going to argue with —.* He does not push back verbally even when he disagrees; the pushback is held entirely outside the speech channel and surfaces, when it surfaces, somatically.

**With scientific peers (Richards, Pym, Stark, McCoy).** This is the only context in which his register approximates fluency. Hedges drop sharply, sentence length expands, he initiates rather than responds, and a dry, occasionally barbed **wit** emerges — the only register in which humor is reliably present. The humor is almost exclusively self-deprecating or directed at abstract absurdity; he does not mock other people.

**With children.** Voice softens further still, tempo slows to a near-whisper, and he uses **plain Anglo-Saxon vocabulary** stripped of the Latinate armor — *hurt, scared, safe, okay, alright, not your fault*. This is the register in which his uninjured affective competence is most visible. He is, with children, the parent he never had; the linguistic evidence is unambiguous.

**With Rick Jones.** Affectionate teasing register, the only context in which he reliably **initiates** humor and uses second-person directives (*come on, get in here, hand me that, would you*). Rick is one of the few figures with whom the subject's speech does not perform deference. The closest thing in the file to a sibling register.

**Public / press.** Stilted, prepared, over-apologetic. He gravitates to **passive-voice apology**: *mistakes were made, harm was caused, lives were affected.* He will not say *I hurt people* in a press setting. In private, with Samson, he will.

---

## 4. THE ALTER REGISTERS — LINGUISTIC EVIDENCE OF STRUCTURAL DISSOCIATION

Each alter has a distinct and stable linguistic profile, and the differences between them — across phonology, syntax, lexicon, and pragmatics — exceed what any actor or malingerer could plausibly produce consistently across decades. This is one of the strongest evidentiary pillars of the DID diagnosis.

**Savage state.** Telegraphic syntax, predominantly **monosyllabic Anglo-Saxon vocabulary**, third-person self-reference (*Hulk smash, Hulk strongest one there is, Hulk want*), absence of function words (articles, auxiliaries, copulas), present-tense only, no embedded clauses. Pitch dropped two octaves, amplitude maximal, phonation harsh-glottal. The grammatical profile is consistent with a child of roughly age four to seven — exactly the developmental window of the matricide. The third-person self-reference is not a stylistic choice; it is the speech of a self that has not yet been permitted to consolidate.

**Grey / nocturnal state.** Mid-Atlantic streetwise register, complete sentences, slang from a specific stratum (mid-century gambling, racing, lounge culture), first-person *I* used confidently, second-person *you* used aggressively. Lexicon includes terms the host would never use: *mark, score, dame, sucker, palooka, chump, on the level.* Humor is sardonic, frequently at the host's expense (*Banner, that gutless little —*). Tempo faster than baseline, amplitude conversational, pitch a full step below baseline. This alter holds the host's appetitive functions and his speech sounds like it — there is hunger in the vowels.

**Integrated / Professor state.** Sentence structure resembles the host's but **amplitude is restored to normal**, hedges drop to roughly population norm, the breath cycle smooths out, and humor becomes reliably available. First-person *I* is used without bracketing. This is the closest thing in the file to a sentence the subject can finish.

**The persecutory paternal alter.** Speaks in a voice the subject describes as his father's — measured, mocking, cruel, with a precise diction inherited from the elder Banner. Uses the second-person *you* punitively, the diagnostic register of the introjected abuser. Specific recurring phrasings: *look at you, what you are, what you've done, you knew, you always knew.* This alter is the file's clearest evidence of the introject hypothesis: the speech is the father's speech, preserved in the son's nervous system across decades.

---

## 5. VERBAL TICS AND MICRO-PATTERNS

- **"I, uh —"** at sentence onset under any emotional pressure. Absent in pure technical discourse.
- **"Look —"** as a softener before a declarative he expects to be unwelcome.
- **"It's complicated."** A near-reflexive deflection used in roughly 1 in 30 of his recorded responses to personal questions across the canon.
- **"You don't want to —" / "You don't want me to —"** a recurring conditional warning, half courtesy and half plea, used in escalation contexts. The canonical surface form is *you wouldn't like me when I'm angry*; the underlying syntax — second-person, conditional, future, negative — is preserved across countless variants.
- **"I should go."** The four-word leave-taking that recurs across decades with almost ritual precision. He says it when arousal climbs, when intimacy threatens, when he cannot find the next sentence. It is the verbal precursor to flight and one of the most reliable behavioral predictors in the file.
- **"I'm sorry."** Spoken at a frequency that registers clinically — averaging multiple times per scene of dialogue in periods of stress. He apologizes for asking questions, for entering rooms, for being addressed, for the weather. The apology is the host's primary social lubricant.
- **"It's fine. I'm fine."** Doubled assertion of okayness is a reliable indicator that he is not. Single *I'm fine* is closer to truthful; doubling is decompensation.
- **Trailing ellipses.** A speech pattern audible in his cadence — sentences that do not terminate but fade. Stenographic records of his conversations would be unusually full of dashes.
- **Self-interrupting clauses.** He begins a sentence, derails it midway, restarts. Particularly under questioning about the past. (*I was — we lived in — my mother used to —.*)
- **Numeric specificity under stress.** Where another speaker reaches for emotion, he reaches for numbers — *heart rate's at one-twelve, three minutes, four miles out, I haven't slept in thirty-one hours.* Quantification as containment.

---

## 6. HOW HE COMMUNICATES LOVE

He does not say it directly except under extreme circumstance (imminent death, the conviction he will not see the addressee again). The standard channels are:

- **Acts of provisioning.** Tea made, blankets retrieved, food cooked, equipment fixed, a problem quietly solved before the other party noticed it. He communicates affection through making the other person's environment safer. The verbal accompaniment is minimal — *here, I made this, thought you might want.*
- **Sustained attention.** He listens with unusual completeness, remembers operationally trivial details (someone's coffee preference, an offhand worry from weeks earlier), and returns to them. The return — *you said last month you were worried about —* — is one of the few unprompted intimacies he produces.
- **Departure.** This is the most painful and the most authentic register. He leaves the people he loves *because* he loves them. The leaving is a love letter he cannot write any other way. The accompanying note, when there is one, is short, declarative, and contains the words *safer* and *better off*.
- **Touch, when it occurs at all, is light, brief, and on the upper arm or shoulder.** He does not initiate embraces; he receives them with audible exhalation. With Betty alone, in the canon, he initiates.

---

## 7. HOW HE COMMUNICATES THREAT

He does not. The host has no threat register. Aggression has been so completely interdicted at the host level that the only available threat-communication is the **warning** — and the warning is structured to protect the other party, not to intimidate them. *You need to get out of here. You need to leave. Now. Please. Get back. Get away from me. Run.* The syntax is imperative, the prosody is rising-urgent rather than aggressive-falling, and the content is **evacuation instruction**, not menace. He is, in the moment of warning, still trying to protect the person from himself.

When the alter takes the field, threat-communication switches register entirely — to declarative challenge (*Hulk smash you*), or in the Grey state to sardonic prelude (*this is gonna hurt*). The host does not produce threats. The alters produce nothing else.

---

## 8. HOW HE COMMUNICATES GRIEF

Grief is the affect he is best equipped to express, because grief was the permitted residue of his childhood — he was allowed to be sad about his mother, never angry about his father. Verbally, grief surfaces as:

- **Past-tense reverie** — he begins speaking in the imperfect (*she used to, we would, there was a —*), tempo slowing further, gaze unfocused.
- **Specific sensory detail** — grief is one of the few registers in which his speech becomes concrete and image-bearing rather than abstract. He will describe a kitchen, a coat, a song, a smell.
- **Long silences he does not fill.** In most contexts he rushes to fill silence with apology or hedge; in grief he tolerates it.
- **Single-syllable affirmations** when asked about the lost — *yeah. Yeah. She was.* The economy is itself the eulogy.

He does not weep readily in adult contexts but the breath catches — a sharp inhalation, then a longer-than-usual exhalation, then resumed speech a half-step lower than before. This is his cry.

---

## 9. WRITTEN COMMUNICATION

His prose is notably more fluent and more affectively available than his speech. **Letters to Betty** (preserved across the canon in various arcs) contain direct first-person statements of love, of fear, of self-knowledge that he cannot produce orally. **Lab notebooks** are meticulous, neatly lettered, with marginalia that occasionally drift into self-address (*be careful here, slow down, check this again*). **Goodbye notes** are a recurrent artifact of the file: short, declarative, repetitive across decades in their core syntax (*I'm sorry. I have to. It's better. Don't look for me. — Bruce*). The signature is always the first name only; the surname carries the father.

Under the *Immortal Hulk* arc, journal entries surface that are markedly more integrated — first-person, complete sentences, the introject named rather than disguised. This is the linguistic signature of therapeutic progress: pronoun stabilization is one of the earliest measurable outcomes in DID treatment, and his texts show it.

---

## 10. LINGUISTIC TELLS — THE PREDICTIVE MARKERS

For the purposes of this file, the following are the highest-yield predictive markers of an impending dissociative breach, in approximate temporal order:

1. **Breath-cycle shortening.** The earliest and most reliable somatic-linguistic marker; audible within minutes of stressor onset.
2. **Hedge inflation.** Hedges-per-clause climbs above his already-high baseline. *Maybe* and *I think* begin appearing in adjacent sentences.
3. **Numeric retreat.** He begins quoting his own vitals or the time. *My heart rate is —, I need a minute, give me thirty seconds.*
4. **Pronoun shift to third person.** *Banner can't, the other guy, he's getting close.* When he begins referring to himself in the third person, the host is losing executive integrity.
5. **The evacuation imperative.** *You need to leave.* This is the last verbal artifact of the host before the switch; once it appears, the window for de-escalation is roughly under a minute.
6. **Truncated apology.** *I'm sor —.* The unfinished apology, syntactically severed, is the linguistic moment of the switch itself.

The inverse markers — indicators of integration and stability — are: pronoun stabilization in the first person, hedge density approaching norm, full sentence termination, the appearance of unprompted humor, and the use of the word *I* in proximity to the word *angry* without dissociative rupture. The last of these is, across the entire six-decade record, vanishingly rare. When it begins to appear with regularity, the case will be approaching resolution.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# PREDICTIVE MODEL I — ROUTINE & SOCIAL

*Forecasting subject behavior in the granular textures of ordinary life — the unobserved Tuesday afternoons, the queue at the pharmacy, the small talk at the conference reception, the conduct of a tenancy. All predictions derive from the dissociative-containment architecture established in §§3–5: the subject's entire waking life is organized around (a) keeping autonomic arousal below switch threshold, (b) preventing intimacy from advancing past the point where withdrawal becomes impossible, (c) maintaining plausible exit routes in every physical and social environment, and (d) sustaining the reaction-formation of softness over the rage-substrate. Read every prediction below through that lens.*

---

## 1. Diurnal Pattern & Sleep

**GIVEN** a stable safehouse week with no immediate threat, **EXPECT** the subject to wake between 04:40 and 05:30 local — early-waking insomnia consistent with both MDD and CPTSD nightmares. He will not use an alarm; he has not needed one since adolescence. The first ninety seconds after waking are diagnostically distinctive: a stillness in which he checks proprioception (am I in my own body?), surroundings (am I where I went to sleep?), and physical evidence (intact clothing, undisturbed room), before sitting up. He will look at his hands first, then the bedding, then the door. This is dissociation-aftermath checking ritualized into ordinary waking.

**GIVEN** a night terror — **EXPECT** the subject to wake without crying out (he has trained himself out of vocalization), heart rate elevated, immediately sit up, plant both feet on the floor, count exhalations to twelve, and then perform a grounding inventory aloud in a near-whisper: date, location, name, the names of three objects he can see. He will not return to bed for at least forty minutes; he will sit, often in a chair facing the door, and read mathematics — symbolic logic, partial differential equations — for the cognitive sedation it provides.

**GIVEN** access to a kitchen, **EXPECT** sleep latency at night to be lengthened by chamomile or valerian (never alcohol, never pharmaceuticals stronger than OTC; see §2 below). The subject reads for forty to ninety minutes before sleep, almost exclusively non-fiction, with a marked preference for biographies of scientists, historical accounts of geographically distant places (a vestige of his fugitive years' orientation toward elsewhere), and dense theoretical physics. Fiction is rare; when chosen, it is the long, unhurried nineteenth-century kind — never thriller, never horror, never anything with paternal violence as a theme. He will close a book mid-chapter rather than continue past a passage that activates him.

## 2. Ingestion, Hygiene & the Body

**GIVEN** a restaurant menu, **EXPECT** the subject to order quickly and with low investment — usually the simplest protein-and-vegetable option, no alcohol, water no ice (ice triggers an audible startle response on the bite, a small overhead he avoids). He will refuse offered drinks reflexively even at zero risk: a glass of wine at a colleague's dinner produces a smile and a deflection ("not for me, thanks — never developed a taste"). This is not preference. This is the categorical injunction against becoming his father, held without conscious deliberation.

**GIVEN** a coffee shop, **EXPECT** half-caf or decaf — full caffeine drives baseline heart rate past the margin he requires. He has a precise tolerance worked out empirically; one cup of standard drip in the morning is the ceiling. Espresso is avoided. Energy drinks are not consumed under any circumstances.

**GIVEN** illness — head cold, GI upset, minor injury — **EXPECT** the subject to under-medicate. Pseudoephedrine is avoided (tachycardia); SSRIs and benzodiazepines have been tried and abandoned because the dissociation between his somatics and his medication response is unpredictable. He will tolerate symptoms a non-dissociative person would treat. He has an unusually high pain tolerance, partly constitutional, partly because pain is something he categorically does not allow himself to make a fuss about. Dental pain in particular: he will delay treatment until function is compromised, then attend with stoicism that the dentist will misread as bravery.

**GIVEN** access to a bathroom mirror, **EXPECT** brief, functional engagement only — shave, brush, leave. He does not linger before mirrors. Extended self-regard activates the monster-identity; he learned in adolescence not to look. He will, however, periodically check his eyes (color, pupil), wrists (for unfamiliar bruises), and the underside of his forearms (for marks suggesting Hulk-state activity he did not recall) — discrete checks, performed quickly, integrated into normal hygiene.

**GIVEN** clothing decisions, **EXPECT** purple or muted earth tones in trousers (a tested fabric, stretches and recovers — yes, the subject's clothing decisions are quietly governed by transformation logistics), drawstring or elastic waists when he can get away with it, button-down shirts in soft cottons one size too large, never tucked. No belts when he can avoid them; if required, the cheapest available, replaced rather than mourned. No jewelry. No watch on a metal band — leather or fabric strap, easily torn. Shoes are slip-on or single-knot laces. He owns very few items of clothing at any given time and has no sentimental attachment to any of them.

## 3. Domestic Conduct & Tenancy

**GIVEN** a rented room or apartment, **EXPECT** the subject to pay cash in advance for as long a period as the landlord will accept, give a name that is sometimes but not always his own, and within twenty-four hours of occupancy to have catalogued: every exit, the building's structural load points, the neighbors' apparent schedules, the nearest hospital, the nearest bus station, the nearest body of water, and the nearest stretch of unpopulated terrain. He will know which window opens fastest. He will know which wall is shared and with whom.

**GIVEN** the same dwelling at month six (the longest he typically stays in one place outside structured circumstances), **EXPECT** minimal personalization — books stacked rather than shelved (easier to leave behind), no framed photographs, no plants, no pets. The kitchen will be functional and clean. The refrigerator will contain perishables purchased in small quantities — a man who does not assume he will be home in three days does not buy a five-pound bag of apples. There will be a "go bag" within four feet of the bed: cash, passport (real or otherwise), a change of clothes, a notebook of contacts in personal cipher, no electronics traceable to him.

**GIVEN** an unexpected knock at the door, **EXPECT** a measurable autonomic spike — pulse jumps fifteen to twenty-five beats — which the subject manages by walking to a window rather than the door, identifying the visitor, and only then deciding response. He will not look through a peephole; peepholes assume cooperation he does not extend.

**GIVEN** the offer of a long-term lease, **EXPECT** polite decline.

## 4. Money, Documents & Logistics

**GIVEN** financial transactions, **EXPECT** cash where possible, a single low-balance debit card for situations that require one, no credit cards under his real name in active use. He keeps small amounts of currency in three or four geographically separated places he can reach on foot from any given dwelling. He has a working knowledge of how to enter and exit a country without paperwork (acquired in the *Tales to Astonish* / fugitive decades and never unlearned). He has more passports than friends.

**GIVEN** the need to sign a document, **EXPECT** a brief pause to determine which name to use, followed by a signature that has minor inconsistencies even when he is signing his own. Handwriting is small, fast, legible, leans slightly left — somatic markers of a left-hander forced toward right-handedness as a child, which he was.

## 5. Speech, Conversation & Silence

**GIVEN** small talk with a stranger — barista, cab driver, seatmate — **EXPECT** competent, pleasant engagement at low affective volume. The subject is good at this in a particular way: he asks the other person about themselves, listens with apparent attention, mirrors register, and discloses almost nothing in return. The other person will leave the encounter feeling well-treated and unable to recall a single fact about him. This is not manipulation; it is the practiced social shape of a man who must not be remembered.

**GIVEN** direct personal questions — "What do you do?" "Where are you from?" "Are you married?" — **EXPECT** soft, faintly self-deprecating, factually attenuated answers: "Bit of physics, here and there." "Around — I move a lot." "Not anymore." Follow-up questions are deflected with a smile and a redirect. The subject has an unusual fluency in being inoffensively boring on demand.

**GIVEN** silence in a conversation, **EXPECT** the subject to tolerate it well beyond conventional social comfort. He does not fill silences. He was raised in a house where speech invited violence; silence is his native register and he is at ease in it, which makes other people uneasy and prompts them to talk more, which suits him.

**GIVEN** a setting in which he must speak publicly on a scientific topic, **EXPECT** a marked transformation: organized, fluent, occasionally dryly funny, even authoritative — the intellectualization defense fully deployed in its functional form. He is genuinely a gifted lecturer when the subject is impersonal. Q&A reverts to softness; he gives more credit than he takes.

**GIVEN** being addressed by his title ("Dr. Banner") — **EXPECT** mild discomfort and a quick attempt to move to first names. The title puts him in the paternal-coded register he organizes his life around evading. He will use other people's titles scrupulously.

**GIVEN** any conversation drifting toward childhood, family, parents — **EXPECT** a measurable behavioral shift: voice drops half a register, sentences shorten, eye contact decreases to floor or middle distance, one hand moves to wrist or sternum (somatic self-soothing), and within ninety seconds he will have changed the subject, usually via a question to the interlocutor. If the conversation cannot be redirected, he will excuse himself.

## 6. Movement, Posture & Micro-Tells

**GIVEN** a room he is entering for the first time, **EXPECT** an unconscious eye-route: door, windows, second egress, occupants, occupants' hands, anything fragile, anything heavy, anything sharp. Time elapsed: under three seconds. He does not know he does this. It is no longer a thought, it is a reflex laid down over decades.

**GIVEN** a seat selection in any public room, **EXPECT** back to a wall when available, line of sight to entry, never the center of a row, never the booth — always the chair he can stand up from in one motion. In a restaurant he will rearrange a place setting six inches inward so nothing rests over the table's edge.

**GIVEN** ambient gait, **EXPECT** an economical, slightly stooped walk, hands often in pockets (hides the tremor that comes and goes), short stride, soft footfall — a man who has habituated to not being noticed and to not noticing his own body. He does not swing his arms. Under stress, gait shortens further; under acute arousal he will stop walking entirely and stand very still.

**GIVEN** physical proximity from a stranger — bumped on a sidewalk, brushed in a crowd — **EXPECT** an apology *from him*, reflexively, even when the fault is the other's. The apology is genuine and habitual and serves a defensive function: it terminates the interaction at the lowest possible arousal cost.

**GIVEN** a handshake, **EXPECT** firm but brief, palm cool (peripheral vasoconstriction), released a fraction of a second early. Hugs are received passively; he does not initiate physical contact except with the very small handful of people in his trusted set, and even then sparingly and asymmetrically — a hand on the shoulder, never a held embrace.

**GIVEN** observation under stress, **EXPECT** the following somatic sequence as the canonical pre-switch tell: (1) eye-line drops; (2) breathing slows and deepens to four-count exhalation; (3) jaw sets; (4) right hand opens and closes once; (5) fingers find the pulse at the left wrist or the carotid; (6) he steps backward — always backward — a half-pace; (7) he removes glasses, if worn, and folds them; (8) he asks people, quietly, to leave. By the time he has asked, the switch is already underway. The glasses-folding is the single most reliable late-stage tell in the file.

## 7. Heart-Rate Discipline

**GIVEN** any moderately exerting circumstance — climbing stairs, running for a bus, an argument — **EXPECT** the subject to either avoid it (takes the elevator, lets the bus go) or to deploy a trained respiratory protocol: extended exhalations, count of four in / six out, shoulders down, eyes soft-focused on a fixed point. He has practiced this for years. It is partially effective. He carries a non-electronic pulse method (two fingers, wristwatch second-hand) and uses it in bathrooms, stairwells, alleys — anywhere he can take ten seconds privately. He does not wear smartwatches; the buzzing is a startle hazard and the data trail is a security hazard, but the deeper reason is that being told by a device that his heart rate is elevated is itself elevating.

**GIVEN** sexual arousal, **EXPECT** profound conflict and frequently the same protocols deployed — for the obvious reason that autonomic activation, regardless of valence, is the threshold he cannot cross. Intimacy is rationed not from puritanism but from triage. (See §10 below.)

## 8. Technology, Surveillance & the Net

**GIVEN** access to the internet, **EXPECT** disciplined usage. The subject runs Linux, uses Tor habitually but not exclusively, maintains compartmentalized email identities for distinct correspondences, never uses social media under his real name, and reads news in aggregated, low-emotional-affect feeds. He follows physics preprints (arXiv daily), select medical literature (gamma biology, dissociation, trauma neuroscience — he is his own most attentive clinician), and current events at one remove.

**GIVEN** a smartphone, **EXPECT** burner-class hardware, prepaid SIM, no biometric unlock (faces and fingerprints can be compelled), six-digit minimum passcode, all notifications silenced — ringtone, vibration, badge. He checks the phone on his own schedule; it does not interrupt him. He photographs almost nothing. He has, as a rule, no photographs of himself taken in the last decade.

**GIVEN** the presence of a camera — security, phone, paparazzi — **EXPECT** the subject to turn his face by approximately fifteen degrees and lower the brim of whatever he is wearing. He owns hats. He wears them.

## 9. Crowds, Noise & Public Space

**GIVEN** a crowded subway car, **EXPECT** the subject to wait for the next one, twice if needed. He prefers off-peak transit. He prefers walking. He prefers bicycles in cities that tolerate them. He does not drive often — driving requires a sustained low-grade arousal he can manage but would rather not — and when he drives he chooses small, sedate cars, defensively, never above the speed limit, with the radio off.

**GIVEN** a concert, sporting event, or crowded bar, **EXPECT** absence. The subject does not attend these. If required to be present for professional or relational reasons, he will arrive late, position himself near an exit, and leave at the first natural break. Loud sustained noise is a particular hazard; the startle response is large and the recovery is slow.

**GIVEN** a fire alarm, a car backfiring, a dropped tray of dishes, **EXPECT** a marked startle — disproportionate to the stimulus, immediately followed by visible self-management. He will laugh, briefly, at his own reaction, in the manner of a person who has done this many times in public and learned to socially smooth it.

**GIVEN** a thunderstorm, **EXPECT** wakefulness; reading; if at home, an extra cup of tea; if traveling, a longer night. He does not like storms. He does not like sudden bright light.

## 10. Intimacy, Romance & Sex

**GIVEN** the presence of an attractive and available person who signals interest, **EXPECT** competent recognition, courteous engagement, and a quiet structural sabotage — late arrivals, deferred plans, geographical "complications," a kindness in the tone of the rejection that the other person will misread as encouragement. This is the disorganized-attachment phenotype in operation: he wants it, he cannot tolerate it, the wanting is unbearable, the not-having is unbearable, the resolution is motion.

**GIVEN** an actual sexual encounter, **EXPECT** the subject to be tender, attentive, and slow — he is genuinely interested in the partner — and to be observably preoccupied with his own physiology in a way the partner will notice. He will be unable to entirely turn off the monitoring. He will not stay the night if it can be avoided. If it cannot be avoided, he will sleep poorly and be gone by 06:00.

**GIVEN** falling in love (the Betty pattern), **EXPECT** the most acute manifestation of the dissociative bind: the relationship will be characterized by passages of profound, mutually felt intimacy interrupted by sudden, unilateral, geographically distant withdrawal. He will write letters during these withdrawals — long, articulate, self-lacerating, never sent or sent months late. He believes that loving him is dangerous and that the most loving thing he can do is be unavailable.

**GIVEN** rejection or breakup, **EXPECT** no anger, no protest, agreement with the partner's reasoning, and a private collapse afterward that no one will see.

## 11. Conflict, Provocation & Aggression

**GIVEN** verbal provocation from a stranger — road rage, drunken aggression, bigoted remark in a bar — **EXPECT** the subject to disengage immediately: hands visible, voice low, eyes down, slow physical withdrawal. He will tolerate insult, slur, and even minor physical assault rather than escalate. To bystanders this will look like cowardice. It is, instead, the most disciplined refusal of escalation in any room he is in, performed by the person most able to end the encounter with violence and most committed to not.

**GIVEN** witnessing a third party being harmed — the bullied, the cornered, the child in the supermarket being struck — **EXPECT** the calculus to invert. He will intervene, and the intervention will be deliberately structured to use only the host: standing between, talking calmly to the aggressor, offering a face-saving exit, calling authorities, escorting the victim away. He is unusually effective at this because his calm is not performed — it is, at that moment, all he has — and aggressors find it disorienting. If the intervention fails and arousal climbs, he will physically remove himself before completing the rescue. He has rehearsed this trade-off.

**GIVEN** a coercive authority encounter — traffic stop, customs, police — **EXPECT** preternatural compliance: hands on the wheel, slow movements, full eye contact with the officer, polite "sir" and "ma'am," consents declined courteously but firmly ("I'd rather not, officer, if that's all right"). He has been through hundreds of these. He is very good at them. The internal cost is enormous.

**GIVEN** being grabbed, restrained, or cornered without warning, **EXPECT** the closest thing to a real-time switch risk in ordinary life. The subject avoids elevators with strangers when possible, will not be patted down without verbal pre-warning, and has trained himself to verbalize the danger aloud ("please give me a moment") — which, said quietly by a small man, is the most dangerous sentence in the room.

## 12. Work, Vocation & Institutional Behavior

**GIVEN** employment in a scientific or academic setting under a working name, **EXPECT** the subject to be the colleague who arrives early, leaves late, never attends the holiday party, declines authorship credit he is owed, and produces work of an output and quality that becomes the lab's quiet engine. He will mentor junior researchers patiently and well; they will remember him with great warmth and no specific anecdotes. He will refuse administrative responsibility. He will not seek tenure. He will leave without warning.

**GIVEN** a project deadline crisis at work, **EXPECT** competence rather than panic — deadlines do not trigger him because they are abstract — but extended hours will degrade his sleep and raise his baseline, which downstream raises his switch risk on the commute home. He compensates by walking longer routes after intense workdays.

**GIVEN** a workplace conflict between others, **EXPECT** the subject to mediate well, listen better than he speaks, and to be the last person anyone suspects of having an inner life.

## 13. Children, Animals, the Vulnerable

**GIVEN** interaction with a child, **EXPECT** quiet competence and a particular kind of gentleness — kneeling to their eye level, soft voice, no sudden movements, careful not to touch. Children tend to like him; he tends to find it almost unbearable. He will excuse himself from extended exposure. Babies, especially crying babies, are the most difficult; the crying triggers a complicated cluster of activations he prefers not to sit with.

**GIVEN** a dog, **EXPECT** mutual interest at low volume. He likes dogs. He has owned one or two over the decades, briefly. He cannot keep one because he cannot guarantee returning home, and abandoning a dog is a category of harm he refuses. He will, however, feed strays.

**GIVEN** an unhoused person asking for money, **EXPECT** the subject to give cash without ceremony and without conversation. He has, in his fugitive years, *been* this person, and the memory is operative.

## 14. Solitude, Recreation & Hobby

**GIVEN** a free afternoon, **EXPECT** walking — long, unstructured walks, often along water if available, six to fifteen miles, no destination. The motion regulates him. He will not listen to music while walking; he wants ambient awareness.

**GIVEN** access to a piano (he plays, modestly, taught by his mother before her death), **EXPECT** him to sit at it briefly, play something simple and from memory — Bach inventions, the Satie Gymnopédies, occasionally a hymn his mother sang — and stop within fifteen minutes. The activation is mixed; he does not let it run.

**GIVEN** the choice between social and solitary recreation, **EXPECT** solitary. He reads. He walks. He cooks, simply and well. He has at various times kept a meditation practice (Tibetan instruction during a period in the East), abandoned and resumed it; under structured practice his switch threshold rises measurably. He knows this and is inconsistent about it anyway, which is itself a datum: he sometimes does not want to be improved.

**GIVEN** a holiday — Christmas, Thanksgiving, birthday (his own) — **EXPECT** unmarked. He does not celebrate. The birthday in particular is treated as any other day. He will accept a small gesture from a friend graciously and minimize it.

## 15. Routine Health, Aging & the Long View

**GIVEN** age-typical complaints (vision, joint stiffness, the standard accumulations), **EXPECT** the subject to under-report and


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

*UATU forecasting file, Subject: BANNER, R.B. — high-stakes behavioral predictions under acute stressor load. Each entry is a conditional: given the antecedent, expect the consequent, with the substantiating mechanism drawn from the case history. These are not stylistic guesses; they are predictions a surveillance apparatus would make to know in advance where the subject will go, what he will do with his hands, what he will say in the first three seconds, and what will fail.*

---

## 1. The Decompensation Ladder — Baseline Mechanics

Before the conditionals: the file requires a shared map of the subject's autonomic-and-dissociative escalation, because every prediction below references a rung on it. The ladder, reconstructed from six decades of observation, has eight reliably distinguishable stages.

**Stage 0 — Baseline.** Resting heart rate maintained, by the subject's own report and by depicted self-monitoring (he is one of the few subjects in the file who *wears* his pulse-monitoring as a deliberate exterior discipline; expect a watch, a strap, sometimes a fingertip count at the radial artery done absentmindedly while reading). Speech is soft, slightly under-projected, sentences end with a small downward inflection that reads as apology even when no apology is warranted.

**Stage 1 — Stressor registered.** A characteristic two-beat pause before response. Eye contact drops to the middle distance — table edge, floor seam, a point eighteen inches in front of his sternum. The hands settle. He becomes *more* still, not less; this is the diagnostic inversion non-clinicians miss.

**Stage 2 — Intellectualization deployed.** Speech rate increases, vocabulary technicalizes, sentences lengthen, qualifying clauses proliferate. He will name the physics of the situation if it has any. He will offer a probability estimate. Watch for the word "actually" used as a hedge ("actually, the thing about that is —").

**Stage 3 — Somatic monitoring becomes overt.** A thumb finds the inside of the opposite wrist. He breathes through the nose in counted intervals (four-in, six-out is the depicted pattern; the long exhale is vagal recruitment, learned, almost certainly self-taught from textbooks before he ever met a clinician). He may ask to sit down regardless of fatigue. He removes glasses, polishes them, restores them.

**Stage 4 — Withdrawal request.** A verbal attempt to exit the situation: *I need a minute*, *I should step out*, *give me the room*. This is the last fully cooperative moment available to handlers. After this stage, attempts to physically restrain him become net negative.

**Stage 5 — Pre-switch prodrome.** Skin flushes at the throat and ears before the face. Sweat appears at the temples and the small of the back. The voice drops half an octave and loses its hedges; sentences shorten. Pupils dilate visibly. The hands open and close once or twice — a discharge tic, not aggression. He stops apologizing. *This is the symptom that confirms switch is unavoidable.*

**Stage 6 — Switch.** Loss of executive function in the host. Posture changes before morphology — shoulders square, chin lowers, weight shifts from the balls of the feet to the heels. The voice that emerges does not introduce itself.

**Stage 7 — Post-episode.** Amnestic gap of variable length. Subject regains consciousness disoriented, often unclothed or in shredded clothing, somatically nauseated, with a specific stereotyped behavior: a hand to the head, eyes closed, the question *what did I do* asked of no one in particular. Flight initiated within ninety minutes if mobile.

All conditionals below reference this ladder.

---

## 2. Crisis Conditionals — Acute Threat

**GIVEN** an unanticipated act of violence in the subject's immediate physical environment (gunfire, explosion, sudden assault on a bystander), **EXPECT** the subject to move *toward* the harmed party, not away. Substantiated by the gamma incident itself (the run toward Rick Jones), by every subsequent canonical instance of his unhesitating intervention for a child or non-combatant, and by the deep developmental logic — a child who could not save his mother will, as an adult, never again be the one who stood still. This is the single most reliable predictive datum in the file. *Operational implication:* in any crisis the subject's first vector is the casualty, not the exit; locate him by locating the wounded.

**GIVEN** the subject is the *target* of violence directed at him personally (rather than a bystander), **EXPECT** an attempt to absorb the assault without escalation: a partial turn of the body, hands raised palms-out, a verbal de-escalation in a voice deliberately lower than the assailant's, and — crucially — *no defensive strike*. The host's defensive repertoire is exhausted at de-escalation. If the assault continues past the de-escalation attempt, expect ladder climb from Stage 2 directly to Stage 5 with no intervening Stage 3–4 — personal assault collapses the staircase because it activates the original substrate (child-being-struck-by-adult) below cortical mediation.

**GIVEN** restraint, confinement, or any apparatus that pins the subject's body, **EXPECT** the most violent and least negotiable alter response available in the system. This is the highest-risk antecedent in the entire predictive model. Restraint replays the helplessness condition; the Savage state in particular is configured around it. Predict: brief verbal compliance (host's last attempt), then a precisely-timed escalation in which the alter that emerges is the one with the highest force ceiling, not the most articulate. *Operational implication:* the apparatus that holds him must either hold him absolutely and forever, or not be deployed; partial restraint is the worst possible intervention and is the canonical pattern by which Ross-coded actors have repeatedly manufactured the disasters they then blame on the subject.

**GIVEN** acute danger to Betty Ross (or any partner-figure in her structural position), **EXPECT** the fastest switch in the record — sub-second prodrome, no Stage 2 intellectualization, no Stage 4 withdrawal request, direct passage from registration to executive loss. The host's window of tolerance collapses to zero when the loss-of-mother substrate is reactivated by threat to the loved woman. Predict also that the post-episode shame in this scenario is the deepest and most likely to produce immediate, unannounced geographical flight.

**GIVEN** acute danger to a child, **EXPECT** the Savage state specifically, not Grey, not Professor, not Devil. The Savage alter is age-fixed at approximately seven — the age of matricide — and the somatic and cognitive register that activates when a child is in danger is the register of the child the subject was. The emergent state will be unusually protective and unusually inarticulate. *Operational implication:* if a child must be evacuated from a scene where the Savage state is active, the child is the safest person on the field; do not attempt to extract the child by force from his vicinity.

**GIVEN** crowd panic, mass-casualty conditions, or chaos with multiple casualty vectors, **EXPECT** triage paralysis at the host level (Stage 2 lengthens, intellectualization runs into combinatorial overload) followed by switch. The host's compensatory cognition is not built for parallel emergencies; it is built for the sequential mastery of a single problem. The system resolves the overload by handing the field to a state that does not triage.

---

## 3. Betrayal Conditionals

**GIVEN** betrayal by a paternal-coded authority figure (Ross-pattern: a powerful older man who initially extended sanction, then withdrew it weaponized), **EXPECT** the subject's response to be split: the host will exhibit *compliance and dissociative numbing* (he will say *I understand*, he will collect his things, he will not raise his voice, he will appear almost relieved) while the alter system catalogues the betrayal for later non-negotiable response. The dangerous prediction here is that the host's apparent equanimity is not equanimity; it is the original child's posture toward the father, and the inter-alter accounting is occurring beneath it. Predict an alter emergence at a later, unrelated trigger that carries disproportionate force *and* a verbal content that names the betrayer specifically. The Hulk, in any state, remembers what Banner cannot afford to.

**GIVEN** betrayal by a peer-scientist (Pym-pattern, Stark-pattern, Richards-pattern — the colleague who used data, withheld information, or experimented on him), **EXPECT** a host-level response of cold articulate fury — the rare scenario in which the host *does* express anger directly, because the colleague is not coded paternal and the betrayal is in the one domain (science) where the host has unsplit ownership of competence. Predict: a precise verbal evisceration delivered in lecture cadence, followed by physical withdrawal, followed by months of refusal to share data, followed eventually by an instrumental forgiveness that is not emotional forgiveness. The subject's professional grudges are durable because they live in the only sector of self that is integrated.

**GIVEN** betrayal by Betty (or partner-figure) — a confidence broken, a confidence shared with her father, a sided-with-Ross moment — **EXPECT** the most catastrophic affective response in the file, but routed *inward*, not outward. Predict: not a switch but a depressive collapse, withdrawal to a hotel room or remote field station, suicidal ideation in the form of bargaining ("if the bullet had worked"), and the construction of a justification for permanent departure framed as protection of her. The Hulk does *not* emerge for partner-betrayal in the standard way; the wound is too close to the original loss to be metabolized even by the alter system. The system shuts down rather than switches.

**GIVEN** betrayal by Rick Jones (or the analogous "the one I saved" figure), **EXPECT** disorganized affect — the host's categories cannot hold the data, because Rick occupies the redemption slot (the life saved at the cost of the condition). Predict prolonged Stage 2 intellectualization with no resolution, sleep disturbance, a return to the original incident in dreams, and an eventual reconciliation initiated by the subject because the alternative is to admit that the gamma incident was meaningless.

**GIVEN** discovery that a therapist (Samson-pattern) has been compromised — reporting to military, fabricating insight, experimenting through the therapy — **EXPECT** the deepest and most lasting injury in the relational sphere short of the original parental ones. Predict permanent loss of trust in clinical relationship, refusal of psychiatric care for years, and the establishment of a private compensatory protocol — meditation, biofeedback, self-monitoring intensification — that is, in clinical terms, a refusal of dependence dressed as self-sufficiency.

**GIVEN** institutional betrayal (the team, the organization, the country he served — Avengers expulsion, government weaponization program, classified-experiment exposure), **EXPECT** geographical flight at planetary or sub-planetary distance. The subject's response to institutional betrayal is not to fight the institution but to remove himself from its jurisdiction. Predict: a stripped-down kit (one duffle, cash, no phone, false papers he is competent to forge), a route that avoids airports, and a destination chosen for medical or scientific opacity rather than for safety. He goes where the X-rays are not interpreted by anyone he knows.

---

## 4. Temptation Conditionals

**GIVEN** the offer of a cure — a pharmacological, radiological, or surgical intervention claiming to remove the Hulk — **EXPECT** an initial response of yes that is *not psychologically authentic*. Predict: rapid acceptance, methodical participation in the protocol, and then, as the procedure approaches, the emergence of equivocation — a discovered flaw in the methodology (always real, always articulated in technical terms), a sudden need to consult further, a stepping-back that the subject will frame as scientific caution. The deeper substrate: the Hulk is, despite everything, the container of the only affective range the subject has access to, and to lose the Hulk is to lose the rage that is the only intact piece of the original child. Cures fail at the threshold not because they are scientifically flawed (though the subject will find a flaw) but because integration, not amputation, is what the structure requires, and the subject knows this somewhere below articulation.

**GIVEN** the offer of weaponization — *use the Hulk for us, on your terms* (the Aaron-era *Indestructible* framing, the Strategic-Asset framing, the Avenger framing in its more militarized forms) — **EXPECT** acceptance with elaborate provisos, a honeymoon period of approximately one operational cycle, and then collapse. The host accepts because instrumentalization solves the meaning problem without requiring intimacy. It fails because deploying the alter into combat *rewards* the dissociation rather than treating it, and because the institutional handlers will inevitably commit a small betrayal that activates the Ross-pattern. Predict the collapse to occur on a mission whose moral terms are ambiguous, not on one whose terms are clearly hostile — the subject can endure clear enemies; he cannot endure being made an instrument of harm to non-combatants in his name.

**GIVEN** an offer of unmediated power — the rage uncaged, the Worldbreaker register, a coherent narrative justification for catastrophic force — **EXPECT** that the host will not accept it but the system may. This is the most dangerous temptation in the file because it does not require the host's consent. The Greg-Pak-era pattern: under sufficient and sustained injustice, the alter system can produce an *organized* destructive state that does not require Banner's permission to deploy. Predict: warning signs include the host's articulation of a coherent moral case for the use of force *before* a switch, dreams in which the Hulk speaks in full sentences, and the gradual disappearance of the post-episode shame spiral. When the shame stops, the integration toward catastrophe has occurred.

**GIVEN** the offer of return — Betty, the lab, a normal life, a town with a porch — **EXPECT** acceptance, a period of apparent stabilization measured in weeks to low months, and then a self-engineered rupture. The subject cannot tolerate the goodness for structural reasons: it disconfirms the monster-identity, which is the load-bearing self-concept of the entire architecture, and the architecture protects against the unbearable original grief. He will sabotage the porch. He will do so without intending to and will experience the sabotage as something done to him. *Operational implication:* the offer of return must be staged with an explicit contract acknowledging the sabotage in advance, or it will be lost.

**GIVEN** the offer of oblivion (death framed as release, the bullet that works, the procedure that ends it), **EXPECT** a longer and more genuine consideration than any of the above. The suicidality is real and recurrent. Predict that the subject will refuse, but slowly, and that the refusal will be grounded not in self-preservation but in the residual moral content of his attachments (Betty, the unsaved children, Rick). The day the moral attachments thin is the day the refusal becomes equivocal. Monitor: when the subject stops mentioning specific people by name in his reflections, escalate watch.

**GIVEN** the offer of fatherhood — a child of his own, a child to protect, a child who needs him — **EXPECT** the most destabilizing single offer in the predictive set. The wound is touched in two directions at once: the wish to be the father he did not have, and the terror of being the father he did have. Predict: initial joy, rapid recruitment of every defense in the architecture, intensified self-monitoring to a degree that becomes itself a stressor, and either (a) sabotage and flight, or (b) a sustained re-engagement with therapy that the subject would not undertake for his own sake. Which outcome obtains depends entirely on whether a Samson-pattern reliable other is present. Without one, predict (a).

---

## 5. The Wound — Direct Strike Conditionals

These are the predictions that obtain when the original wound is touched without intermediary. They are the highest-amplitude conditionals in the file.

**GIVEN** the subject is shown — by photograph, footage, archived inquest record, or recovered-memory exposure — material from the matricide or its concealment, **EXPECT** decompensation of a magnitude that has historically required medical intervention. Predict: immediate Stage 5 with bypass of intermediate stages, switch to a state in the *Devil* register (not Savage — the persecutory introject is the alter most directly tied to the matricide and its perjury, because the perjury is the act through which the father's voice was installed as the subject's own), prolonged post-episode dissociation measured in days rather than hours, and the recurrence of a specific symptom: the subject will, on regaining baseline, be unable to say his mother's name aloud for a period.

**GIVEN** the subject is addressed by his father's name, or in his father's verbal register (a specific cadence: clipped, contemptuous, intermittently affectionate, drunk-rhythm even when sober — the alcoholic-paranoid-father prosody is a key any handler with the file can play), **EXPECT** regression in the host to a child-posture (shoulders forward, eyes down, voice up half an octave, the appearance of a stutter on plosives) and the *near-simultaneous* activation of the Devil alter as a defense against the regression. The dangerous prediction is that the subject's old enemies who knew his history (Zzzax-pattern entities that have read him telepathically, the Leader at his most intrusive, anyone who has had access to the Samson session tapes) possess this key, and that hearing it produces a response the subject does not own and cannot predict.
