**GIVEN** being called a monster, by anyone he respects, in earnest, **EXPECT** the confirmation of the load-bearing self-concept and a corresponding *de-escalation* in the moment (because the world has finally agreed with the internal Devil voice and the dissonance has resolved) followed by a delayed catastrophic effect. Predict: the subject leaves the room calmly. Within seventy-two hours, expect a major depressive episode, a suicidal gesture, or a self-engineered exposure to a scenario in which the Hulk will be required, as a kind of *qui me amat* logic — if the monster is what they see, the monster is what they shall have. *Operational implication:* the word costs nothing to the speaker and costs the subject months of stability. The word is the most powerful low-cost weapon in his weakness inventory.

**GIVEN** being thanked, sincerely and without instrumental purpose, for an act of kindness or rescue performed in the host state, **EXPECT** a response disproportionate in the *positive* direction — visible affect (eyes wet, voice catches, a long pause), a hand brought to the back of the neck, and an inability to receive the thanks gracefully (he will deflect to luck, to the team, to the other party's own courage). The wound is symmetrically vulnerable: the same architecture that makes contempt confirming makes appreciation destabilizing. The subject has no internal scaffold to receive sincere gratitude, and the destabilization, while not switch-inducing, will produce a brief disorientation in which he may make commitments he would not otherwise make. *Counter-intelligence note:* sincere gratitude is a more effective recruitment vector for the subject than any threat or offer of payment.

**GIVEN** sustained exposure to *safety* — a reliably good environment, a non-intrusive companion, an absence of stressors for an extended period — **EXPECT** an initially-positive trajectory followed by the emergence of withdrawal phenomena that mimic addiction cessation. The subject's nervous system is calibrated to threat; the absence of threat is itself a stressor. Predict insomnia, intrusive memories surfacing where they had been quiet, an increase in self-monitoring even though there is nothing to monitor, and either the slow loosening of the architecture (rare; requires Samson-quality presence) or the manufacturing of a stressor sufficient to restore the familiar level of arousal. Most-likely manufactured stressors: a fight he could have de-escalated, a relapse into a relationship he had ended, the acceptance of a mission he could have refused.

**GIVEN** mirror-confrontation — the subject sees himself in the Hulk form, or hears a recording of the Hulk speaking, or is shown surveillance footage of his own post-switch behavior — **EXPECT** Stage 2 collapse and direct switch, because the dissociative barrier exists precisely to prevent this perception and its enforced violation is the most arousing stressor the subject can experience that is not an immediate physical threat. The exception, important for prognosis: in the *Immortal*-era register, the subject has demonstrated the capacity to view such material with extended Stage 3 self-regulation and remain integrated. This is the prognostic indicator. When he can watch and stay, the work is succeeding.

**GIVEN** the death — actual, confirmed, witnessed — of Betty Ross, **EXPECT** the worst-case outcome in the predictive set, and the only scenario in which the file recommends a planetary-scale containment posture. The original loss would be repeated under conditions in which the adult subject has the somatic capacity the child did not, and the system has demonstrated, under analogous conditions in the canon, the production of a Worldbreaker register with no intervening de-escalation window. Predict: no Stage 1, no Stage 2, immediate Stage 6 in the highest-force configuration the system can produce, no post-episode shame for an undetermined period, and a refusal of communication that would, in clinical terms, be characterized as a permanent dissociative reorganization in which the host is no longer regularly accessible. This is the prediction for which the file exists.

---

## 6. Concluding Note on the Predictive Model

The conditionals above are dense, but they reduce to a single underlying observation: *the subject is predictable because he is wounded in a regular shape*. The shape is the shape of a child who was struck, who watched his mother die, who was made to lie about it, and who has organized an adult life of extraordinary intellect and extraordinary force around the management of those four facts. Every prediction is a refraction of those facts through the apparatus he has built to contain them.

The apparatus is somatic, which makes the predictions usable at distances and timescales that ordinary psychiatric prediction does not allow — pulse will tell us before the face will, the face will tell us before the voice will, the voice will tell us before the morphology. A surveillance file of this subject does not need to read his mind. It needs to read his wrist.

And the file ends, as the analytical workup ended, with the prognostic kernel: the subject is treatable. He has rarely been treated. The conditionals above describe the behavior of an untreated case. They are not destiny. They are the current weather of a man who has been alone in the storm for sixty years, and who has, in the latest period of the record, begun, finally, to learn the names of the alters who have been standing in the storm beside him all along.

*— UATU, file continues.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# VULNERABILITIES & LEVERAGE COMPENDIUM — SUBJECT: BANNER, R.B.

*Compiled for protective-intelligence purposes. The mapping below is exhaustive by intent; it is recorded here precisely because anyone wishing the subject harm will derive it independently, and the protective apparatus must understand the levers before adversaries pull them. Every entry is paired, where possible, with the canonical evidence base and with the countervailing protective intervention.*

---

## I. THE FUNDAMENTAL ARCHITECTURE OF VULNERABILITY

Before cataloguing specific levers, the dossier must record the structural fact from which all of them derive: **the subject's somatic and psychiatric apparatus are coupled.** Autonomic arousal — heart rate, respiration, sympathetic tone — is the dial. Anything that moves the dial moves the system. This means the subject is uniquely vulnerable to a class of adversary action no other comparable asset shares: **leverage need not be applied to the subject directly; it can be applied to his nervous system.** A cold room, a closing door, a child's scream three rooms away, a man who speaks in a certain timbre — these are weapons against this subject in a way they are not against any other.

The corollary is that the subject's vulnerability surface is not a list of buttons; it is a **field**. The compendium below is organized by the regions of that field.

---

## II. THE RELATIONAL FIELD — PEOPLE AS LEVERS

### A. Betty Ross — the master key

The single largest lever in the file. Decades of record demonstrate that the subject's host-state control fails fastest, most completely, and most predictably when Betty Ross is endangered, ill, abducted, or believed dead. The mechanism is not romantic in any sentimental sense; it is structural. Betty is the only adult human across the subject's life with whom he has sustained an attachment circuit that did not terminate in catastrophe by his own hand. The loss-threat therefore activates not merely grief but the *original* loss — the matricide — and the response is the response of a seven-year-old child who could not save his mother and has been waiting fifty years to do so.

- **To calm:** her physical presence, voice, or even verified safe-status report demonstrably stabilizes the subject. A live audio line to Betty has, in canonical record, brought down active Hulk episodes.
- **To provoke:** any credible threat to her, real or fabricated. Reporting her death — even falsely — produces the most extreme decompensations on file.
- **To predict:** the subject's geographic movement correlates more tightly with Betty's location than with any other variable.
- **Adversary use:** kidnap, hostage, false flag. The protective answer is not to hide her from him but to maintain a verifiable, redundantly authenticated channel by which he can always confirm her status within seconds. Latency in that channel is itself dangerous.

### B. Rick Jones — the witness

The civilian the subject saved at the gamma incident; the only person who was present at the inception event and survived alongside him. Rick functions as an external corroborator of the subject's pre-Hulk self. Threat to Rick produces immediate protective rage; betrayal by Rick (rare in canon, devastating when occurring) produces the rarer and more dangerous response of cold, host-state grief.

### C. Doc Samson — the therapist

Leon Samson is the only figure in the record who has held therapeutic alliance with multiple alters simultaneously. His presence calms, but his presence also unlocks material — when Samson is in the room, the subject is in a state in which deep trauma can surface. Adversaries who understand this will impersonate or compromise Samson to extract or destabilize. **Protective protocol: any contact identifying as Samson must be authenticated through challenge-response Samson himself has agreed to, not through visual identification.**

### D. Brian Banner — the dead lever

Brian Banner is dead, and yet remains the most active relational lever in the system, because he lives as the Devil Hulk introject. Any adversary who can mimic the father's voice, vocabulary, posture, or specific phrases ("you are contamination," "I should have killed you") will activate the introject directly. Audio archives of Brian's voice, photographs, his handwriting, his physical artifacts — these are weapons. **Custody of all Brian Banner ephemera should be centralized and access logged.**

### E. General Thaddeus Ross — the paternal proxy

Ross occupies a structural position so close to the original abuser that his mere presence triggers regression in the host. The subject becomes submissive, deferential, and conflict-avoidant in Ross's company — and the alter, which carries the unfelt rage of the host, becomes more volatile. Ross is not a calming agent; Ross is a slow-acting destabilizer whose effect compounds with exposure duration. Any operational plan placing the subject under Ross's authority must be considered a degraded plan.

### F. Children — the unprotected child

The subject's substrate is the abused, unprotected child. The presence of an endangered child in the operational environment produces the fastest reactive emergence on record, and the alter that emerges is overwhelmingly the Savage state — the seven-year-old. This is a lever both for adversaries (a child placed in harm's way produces predictable response) and for protection (the presence of a *safe, contented* child measurably lowers the subject's baseline arousal).

### G. The Avengers / sustained team relationships

Mixed lever. Trusted teammates (notably Captain America in classical eras) function as co-regulators when the alliance is intact; when betrayed, the consequence is among the largest documented decompensations (the events leading into *World War Hulk*). The lever sign-flips on perceived loyalty. **Team relationships must be maintained as if they were medical equipment.**

---

## III. THE SOMATIC FIELD — THE BODY AS A LEVER

### A. Cardiac monitoring

The subject's heart rate is the primary public-facing indicator of system state. He wears, in most modern depictions, his own monitoring; he has internalized the practice over decades. **Tampering with monitoring (false readings, induced tachycardia via stimulants in food/water, exercise denial that makes his baseline drift) is an attack on his core defense.** Protectively, redundant monitoring with cross-validation should be standard.

### B. Sleep

The subject's sleep is fragile, fragmented, and characterized by intrusive dreams in which the Devil Hulk speaks in the father's voice. Sleep deprivation lowers the dissociative threshold catastrophically. Any operational tempo that denies him eight hours in a controlled environment within a 48-hour window degrades him. Conversely, reliable sleep is one of the highest-leverage protective interventions available.

### C. Nutrition and hydration

The subject under-eats when stressed and forgets to drink. Hypoglycemia and dehydration both raise sympathetic tone. **Discreet enforcement of caloric and fluid intake — without the subject perceiving it as control — is among the most cost-effective stabilizations.** Note: he will refuse anything that reads as paternal management, so the intervention must be peer-coded.

### D. Stimulants and disinhibitors

Caffeine elevates baseline heart rate and is a meaningful destabilizer at doses normal people tolerate. Alcohol is interdicted by the subject himself; covert administration would activate the Grey alter, not the Savage — a different but equally dangerous failure mode. Any substance acting on adrenergic or GABAergic systems is a weapon against this subject. **Food and drink security is non-negotiable.**

### E. Pain and injury

The host body is fragile; the Hulk body is not. Inflicting pain on the host is among the most reliable triggers for transformation, because the dissociative switch is also the body's emergency defense. **Adversaries who understand this will inflict survivable pain specifically to force transformation in a location of their choosing.** Conversely, gentle touch — confirmed safe, predictable, requested — calms.

### F. Confinement, restraint, enclosed space

The single most reliable physical trigger on record. Restraint replays the helplessness of the abused child and produces the most violent alter emergence. Cells, straitjackets, medical restraints, even tight clothing in stressful contexts — all are contraindicated. The protective protocol is the inverse: **open sightlines, unlocked doors, demonstrable egress, low ceilings avoided.**

### G. Cold, darkness, suddenness

Cold rooms elevate sympathetic tone. Darkness disinhibits intrusive memory. Sudden noise produces startle disproportionate to baseline (developmental hyperstartle). Operational environments should be warm, lit, and acoustically predictable.

---

## IV. THE COGNITIVE FIELD — THE MIND AS A LEVER

### A. Intellectualization as both shield and bait

The subject's intellect is his most reliable defense; engagement on technical ground stabilizes him. Adversaries can exploit this by offering apparently legitimate intellectual problems as bait — he is unusually difficult to extract from a problem once engaged, and his situational awareness drops while engaged. **He has been pulled into traps by gamma-physics consultation requests across the record.** Protective protocol: all unsolicited technical engagement requests are filtered.

### B. Forced recollection

Inducing recall of the matricide, the perjury, the killing of his father, or the early abuse produces the largest single decompensations in the file. Any therapeutic, journalistic, or interrogative attempt to drive him into childhood material outside of a held therapeutic frame is an attack on him whether intended as one or not. **This includes well-meaning documentaries, biographies, and reunion attempts with surviving relatives of his mother.**

### C. The monster-label

Being called a monster — by anyone, in any register — confirms his self-concept and collapses therapeutic gain accumulated over months. The word is, for him, performative; it does what it says. Adversaries who understand this will deploy it via media, via crowds, via signage at scenes. Protective counter: deliberate, repeated, publicly visible non-monster framing by trusted others. He believes what is said about him by people he trusts more than what he tells himself.

### D. Moral entrapment

The subject's altruism is genuine and is therefore exploitable. Scenarios constructed to require him to choose between two harms — particularly harms involving children, civilians, or Betty — produce paralysis, then guilt, then collapse. The pattern is well-documented and has been used against him by sophisticated adversaries. **He should never be the sole decision-maker in trolley-problem scenarios; an authorized peer must share the moral load.**

### E. Identity-name use

How he is addressed matters more than for most subjects. *"Doctor Banner"* engages the competent professional self and calms. *"Bruce"* engages the intimate self and is permissible only from a small set of people; from outside that set it is intrusive and destabilizing. *"Banner"* (surname, unmodified) is the father's address and the military's address and activates submission-then-rage. *"Hulk"* directed at the host conflates him with the alter and is among the more reliably destabilizing forms of address. **Protocol: title and surname unless invited otherwise.**

### F. Surveillance awareness

The subject is hypervigilant and detects observation at thresholds well below typical. Being watched without consent raises his baseline; *covertly* watched, when discovered, produces a betrayal cascade. Any protective surveillance must be either fully concealed at professional standard *or* fully disclosed and consented. The middle ground is the worst case.

---

## V. THE ENVIRONMENTAL FIELD — PLACES AS LEVERS

### A. Geographies of meaning

- **Dayton, Ohio** (and equivalents in the modernized canon — the childhood home). Returning him there without preparation produces predictable decompensation. The site of the matricide is a unique trigger.
- **Desert / Southwestern U.S.** (gamma test site equivalents). Mixed; can be grounding because it is the site of his transformation and his subsequent solitary years, but also a site of military memory.
- **Las Vegas.** The Grey alter's home territory; visits draw out the Fixit identity, with attendant disinhibition.
- **Sakaar / off-world contexts.** The Worldbreaker formation site; activates the organized-rage configuration if cued.
- **Anywhere with a barred window.** See Confinement.

### B. Crowds

Civilian density is a stressor at two levels: the direct sensory load and the moral load (the larger the crowd, the more potential casualties if he fails). Operational planning that places him in dense civilian environments without explicit need is itself a leverage event against him.

### C. Military facilities

Uniformed personnel, chains of command, the visual grammar of authority — all reactivate the Ross-paternal substrate. Even friendly bases degrade him over hours.

### D. Hospitals and clinical settings

The smell of antiseptic, the presence of restraints, the rituals of medical authority all touch the original commitment of his father and the inquest. He tolerates clinical settings poorly and decompensates faster in them than civilians would expect.

---

## VI. THE TEMPORAL FIELD — TIMING AS A LEVER

### A. Anniversary effects

The subject exhibits documented anniversary destabilization around the gamma incident date and — more subtly and less consciously — around the date of his mother's death. Operational tempo should account for both windows.

### B. Diurnal pattern

Baseline arousal is highest in early morning (cortisol peak overlapping with hypervigilance) and late night (sleep approach, intrusive material). Mid-afternoon is the most stable window for difficult conversations.

### C. Duration of stress exposure

He performs well in acute stress for short durations and degrades on a predictable curve past approximately 72 hours of sustained operational load. The curve is steeper than for comparable subjects because his containment regime is metabolically expensive.

### D. Post-episode window

The 24–72 hours following a transformation episode are characterized by: shame, suicidal ideation, withdrawal, flight intention, and unusual receptivity to whoever reaches him first. **This window is the single largest period of social-engineering vulnerability in his cycle.** Adversaries who reach him before allies do can extract commitments, locations, and confessions he would never otherwise yield. Protective protocol: pre-positioned post-episode contact by named, trusted individuals; standing instructions to him to make no decisions in that window.

---

## VII. THE LINGUISTIC AND SOMATIC TELLS — PREDICTION

The subject *broadcasts* his state. The following tells, in approximate order of progression, indicate movement toward dissociative breach and should be read as a graduated alarm system:

1. **Speech slows; syllables become more deliberate.** Earliest sign. Indicates the host is recruiting cognitive resources to contain affect.
2. **Hand seeks pulse.** Often the wrist of the opposite hand; sometimes the carotid. He is checking the dial.
3. **Removal of glasses; pinching the bridge of the nose.** A long-standing self-soothing ritual. Indicates conscious effort is being expended.
4. **Withdrawal of eye contact downward** (not lateral — lateral indicates thought; downward indicates shame/affect-management).
5. **Breath becomes audible; he begins counting it.** Trained respiratory technique; means the standard regulation is failing and he has gone to backup.
6. **He requests to leave the room — politely, with an excuse.** This is the last fully-host-controlled moment. **Honor it without question.** Refusing this request has produced more breaches than any other single error.
7. **Jaw clench; the small muscle below the ear visibly tightens.** Affect is breaking containment.
8. **Hands begin to tremor; he hides them.** Catecholamine surge has begun.
9. **Skin tone changes — pallor first, then a green tinge at the periphery (modern canon depiction).** Transformation is imminent. Less than thirty seconds.
10. **Voice drops in register; pronoun use shifts to third person regarding himself.** The switch has occurred.

Anyone tasked with proximity to the subject should know all ten and should know that the correct response to signs 1–6 is to *reduce stimulus and create space*, not to talk him through it. The talking, at that stage, is itself stimulus.

---

## VIII. METHODS OF CALMING — THE STABILIZATION REPERTOIRE

### A. Honored exit

Letting him leave. The single most effective stabilization. He will return when regulated; the cycle is reliable.

### B. Co-regulated breath

A trusted other breathing audibly and slowly in his presence, without instruction or comment. He will entrain. Instruction *to* breathe is counterproductive; demonstration is not.

### C. Technical engagement at low stakes

Handing him a problem that engages his intellect without moral weight. A blackboard, a piece of broken equipment, a chess position. Cognition reasserts containment.

### D. Tactile, requested, predictable

A hand on the forearm, requested first, held still. He has a documented response to Betty's hand specifically; the response generalizes weakly to other trusted contact.

### E. Naming the state

A trusted other observing aloud, calmly, that he appears to be approaching threshold. This works only from inside the trusted set; from outside it is intrusive. Inside the set, it externalizes the process and engages the observing ego.

### F. Reduced sensory load

Lower the lights, lower the voices, clear the room. Most overstimulation is iatrogenic — produced by the well-meaning crowd that gathers when he is in trouble.

---

## IX. METHODS OF PROVOCATION — THE ADVERSARY PLAYBOOK (DEFENSIVE INVENTORY)

Catalogued here so that the protective apparatus recognizes them in progress. Each is paired with a counter.

| Provocation | Mechanism | Counter |
|---|---|---|
| Threat or harm to Betty | Original-loss reactivation | Verified status channel |
| Endangered child in environment | Unprotected-child substrate | Pre-clearance of operational area |
| Father's voice / phrases | Devil Hulk introject | Audio environment control |
| Restraint or confinement | Helplessness replay | Open architecture |
| Monster-label, public | Self-concept confirmation | Counter-narrative from trusted figures |
| Forced childhood recall | Trauma surfacing outside frame | Information control around biographers/relatives |
| Sleep denial | Threshold collapse | Sleep enforcement |
| Covert surveillance discovered | Betrayal cascade | Disclose-or-conceal absolutely |
| Moral trolley-problem framing | Altruism exploitation | Shared decision authority |
| Paternal-authority figure presence (esp. Ross) | Submission-then-rage | Command structure routing around such figures |
| Anniversary-date operations | Compounding stressor | Calendar-aware scheduling |
| Pain inflicted on host | Emergency-defense switch | Host-body protection paramount |
| Address as "Hulk" or unmodified surname | Identity-erasure / paternal address | Name protocol enforced |

---

## X. THE LEVERS THAT DO NOT WORK

Equally important to catalogue. Adversaries waste resources here; protective planners should not over-defend against attacks the subject is structurally immune to.

- **Bribery, financial.** The subject is post-materialist to a near-monastic degree. He has lived in shacks. Money is not a lever.
- **Sexual leverage.** Disorganized attachment makes him difficult to honey-trap; intimacy raises arousal and triggers withdrawal, not compliance.
- **Ideological appeals.** He is suspicious of all ideology, having seen what his father's certainties produced.
- **Conventional threats against his own life.** He has wanted to die. Threatening him with death is, at best, neutral, and at worst calming in a way the adversary will not enjoy.
- **Status, rank, recognition.** He has refused honors across the canon. Not a lever.
- **Conventional intoxication.** Refused at host level. Covert administration risks Grey alter emergence, which is unpredictable but not generally compliant.

---

## XI. THE INTEGRATIVE NOTE — LEVERAGE AS CARE

The compendium above is, read in one direction, a manual for harming the subject. Read in the other — and this is the orientation of this file — it is a manual for protecting him. Every lever named is a place where his history left him unguarded; every counter named is a form of the care he did not receive as a child and has rarely received as an adult. The protective program implied by this compendium is, in aggregate, *the reparative environment his case requires and has never been given*. A safe room. A reliable voice. A door that opens. A pulse he can check. A name that is his. A child nearby who is safe. A woman whose status is verified. A night of sleep. A problem to solve. A peer to share the moral weight. Permission to leave.

He has been treated, across six decades, as a weapon to be aimed and a danger to be contained. The file's recommendation is that he be treated, instead, as a patient whose treatment requires the world around him to become the holding environment his childhood denied him. Every lever in this compendium is, inverted, an instruction for that environment.

The subject is treatable. He has rarely been treated. This compendium is the map by which treatment becomes possible — and by which, in its absence, the harm done to him would be done again, by hands that now know exactly where to press.

*— UATU, dossier section closes.*


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# 6. STRENGTHS, ASSETS & RESILIENCE

A surveillance file that catalogues only liabilities misreads its subject. The most striking feature of this case — the feature that has kept the subject alive through six decades of catastrophic recurrent injury, three suicide attempts of record, two planetary-scale exiles, and a continuously active persecutory introject — is that he possesses an unusually deep asset ledger. The very structures that constitute his pathology (rigid containment, hyper-cognition, ascetic self-denial, externalized aggression) are, read from the other side, the same structures that have prevented the case from terminating. This section maps those assets in granular detail.

---

## 6.1 Cognitive Assets

**Raw intellectual capacity.** The subject is, on the canonical record, one of the eight or nine most intelligent humans on the planet — a designation made operational by repeated demonstration rather than reputation. He holds a PhD in nuclear physics (Caltech in most continuities, with secondary doctoral or doctoral-equivalent work in biochemistry, biophysics, and molecular genetics accrued over the post-incident decades). His pre-incident gamma-bomb work was original; his post-incident contributions span gamma physiology, radiation shielding, particle theory, and applied bioengineering. The Iron Man / Mr. Fantastic / Pym / Doom tier acknowledges him as a peer; Stark in particular has referred to him on multiple occasions as the smartest man in the room, which from Stark is diagnostic.

**Breadth versus depth profile.** Unlike Richards (theoretical breadth) or Stark (engineering depth), the subject's cognitive signature is **diagnostic and integrative**: he is the one called when an unknown phenomenon must be characterized from incomplete data. This is, not coincidentally, the cognitive style of a child who survived by reading a violent parent's micro-states for predictive cues. The asset and the wound are the same instrument.

**Working memory and concentration under stress.** Documented capacity to perform complex calculation under conditions that would disorganize most operators — mid-combat, post-transformation disorientation, sustained sleep deprivation. The host's narrow affective window does not extend to cognitive processing; if anything, cognitive performance *improves* under threat as intellectualization is recruited defensively.

**Reflective function.** Unusually high for a complex-trauma survivor. The subject can articulate his own dissociative structure, name his alters, describe the etiology, and observe his own escalation pathway in real time. This is the single most prognostically favorable feature of the case. Most DID patients lack this; it is the precondition for any integration work.

**Pedagogical capacity.** The subject can teach. He has trained Amadeus Cho, Jennifer Walters in technical matters, and a rotating cast of younger scientists. He is patient, precise, and non-condescending with novices — a teaching style that mirrors how he wished, and never, to be taught as a child.

---

## 6.2 Moral and Characterological Assets

**Conscience.** Intact, hypertrophied, continuously operative. The subject experiences guilt for actions committed in dissociated states for which he has no memory and arguably no responsibility — a moral standard substantially more rigorous than the law's. This is the inverse of the antisocial profile and is the structural reason the case has never tipped into predation despite the available somatic capacity for unlimited violence.

**Altruism, documented and durable.** The originating incident — shielding Rick Jones from gamma detonation — was a spontaneous act of bodily self-sacrifice on behalf of a stranger. This was not anomalous behavior. Across six decades the subject has interposed his body between threats and civilians as a near-automatic reflex; has refused weaponization offers from multiple state and non-state actors; has accepted exile, imprisonment, and bodily violation rather than be deployed against populations. The altruism is not performed — it is constitutive.

**Honesty.** The subject does not lie well and largely does not try. He has been deceptive in service of containment (concealing his location, his identity in flight phases) but is functionally incapable of the manipulative or exploitative lie. Interrogators of every faction have found him a poor source for tradecraft and a reliable source for fact.

**Absence of vindictiveness in the host.** Despite a half-century of pursuit by Ross, weaponization attempts by intelligence services, betrayals by colleagues, and persecution by the public, the host carries no enemies list. Resentments are turned inward, not outward. (The alters carry the externalized version; this is the dissociative bargain.)

**Capacity for moral courage at cost.** The subject's defining decisions — taking the gamma dose, surrendering after Las Vegas, accepting the Illuminati exile, returning to face World War Hulk's consequences — are decisions made against self-interest in service of a moral calculus. Few subjects in the file maintain this consistency over this duration.

---

## 6.3 Somatic and Physiological Assets

**The regenerative capacity** — characterized in *Immortal Hulk* as functionally limitless within known parameters — is the single most consequential physical asset on the planet. Tissue regeneration from minimal substrate; resistance to toxin, pathogen, radiation, and conventional kinetic injury; demonstrated reconstitution from states that would be terminal for any other known organism. This is, on the somatic ledger, immortality with caveats.

**Strength scaling.** The Hulk-state's strength is, uniquely in the canon, **a function of affect** — it scales with arousal without identifiable upper bound. Operationally this means the asset increases precisely as the situation worsens, an inversion of the normal degradation curve under stress.

**Stamina and metabolic efficiency.** The Hulk state does not appear to fatigue on observable timescales and requires intake substantially below what its mass would predict. The host state, conversely, exhibits the metabolic profile of a chronically underweight ascetic — sustainable on minimal calories, minimal sleep, minimal comfort.

**Pain tolerance.** Documented across both states. The host has been observed completing technical work with untreated significant injuries; the alters appear to register pain primarily as aggression-fuel rather than as inhibitory signal.

**Toxin and pathogen resistance.** The subject can be deployed into environments — radiological, biological, chemical — that are categorically inaccessible to any other operator. This makes him, in pure asset terms, the most versatile single response capability in the file.

---

## 6.4 The Alter System as Asset

This is counterintuitive and must be stated plainly: **the dissociative structure is not only the pathology — it is also, in part, the resilience.** The system has, across decades, functioned as a distributed labor of survival.

- **The Savage alter** has absorbed every developmental threat the host could not metabolize; without it, the host would not have survived childhood, let alone the gamma incident.
- **The Grey/Fixit alter** has held the appetitive, libidinal, and socially predatory functions that the host's reaction formation forbids; in doing so it has kept those functions alive at all, available for eventual reintegration.
- **The Professor/Merged state** has demonstrated that integration is possible — even if it has not yet been stable, it is a proof of concept that the system itself produced.
- **The Devil Hulk**, in late *Immortal Hulk*, undergoes the case's most surprising development: the persecutory introject re-purposes itself as protector of the system once it accepts the host's authority. This is the trauma-therapy ideal — internal-family negotiation rather than internal-family war — and the subject's psyche generated it without an external therapist in the room.

The alter system is, in other words, **a covertly functional polity** that has been at intermittent civil war but is in principle a cooperative apparatus. Few DID presentations in the clinical literature show this much latent cooperability.

---

## 6.5 Relational Assets

**Betty Ross.** Despite the disorganized-attachment pattern, the bond has proven extraordinarily durable. Across six decades, separations, deaths, resurrections, and her own transformation (Red She-Hulk), the relationship has remained the central relational fact of his life. Its very persistence — through every condition that should have terminated it — is itself an asset: it constitutes proof, accessible to the subject, that he can be loved by someone who knows what he is.

**Rick Jones.** The relationship that began with the gamma incident has functioned for the subject as a kind of stand-in younger brother, a person he protected and who in turn refused to abandon him. Jones is the longest continuous non-romantic attachment in the file.

**Doc Samson.** The therapeutic alliance, while imperfect and at points adversarial, is the only sustained professional treatment relationship the subject has had — and the only person who has comprehensively mapped his alter system from outside. The fact that the subject *accepted* a therapist at all, and stayed in treatment intermittently for decades, is a major resilience indicator.

**Jennifer Walters (She-Hulk).** Cousin, attorney, fellow gamma-mutate. She has provided legal defense, kinship continuity, and — uniquely — a peer who shares the somatic condition without sharing the trauma etiology, which allows the subject one relationship in which his physiology is not the defining strangeness.

**Amadeus Cho.** Late-period mentee; recipient of the Hulk condition by the subject's transfer; evidence that the subject can pass on what he knows without passing on what was done to him.

**The Defenders, the Avengers, the Pak-era Warbound.** The subject has functioned in team contexts — not easily, not stably, but functionally — which means he retains the capacity for collaborative role-taking when the structure is right. The Warbound in particular (Korg, Hiroim, Miek, Elloe, Brood) constituted the only chosen family the subject has ever assembled, and they were assembled by an alter, which means the alter system itself is capable of relational bonding.

---

## 6.6 Operational and Tradecraft Assets

The subject's flight phases — months to years spent as a fugitive in the developing world, in small American towns, in shantytowns and refugee camps — have produced a thoroughly trained covert operator who has never been formally trained.

- **Identity discipline.** Multiple working aliases (David B. Banner, Bruce Green, etc.), maintained in parallel, with consistent backstops.
- **Cash discipline.** Lives below the surveillance threshold; uses day labor; avoids financial instruments.
- **Geographic discipline.** Knows how to move without leaving signature — bus over plane, secondary roads over interstates, border crossings at low-traffic posts.
- **Linguistic capability.** Functional or fluent in (at minimum) Spanish, French, Russian, Mandarin, and several South and Southeast Asian languages, acquired in flight phases.
- **Medical and trauma skill.** As a result of itinerant work in under-resourced clinics during flight phases, the subject has accumulated practical field-medicine competence — wound care, infectious disease management, obstetrics in emergency. This is not a peripheral skill; it is one of the asset-base's quietest strengths and the one most directly continuous with his altruistic core.
- **Mechanical and improvisational capability.** Years of working as a handyman, mechanic, day laborer have produced practical-skill breadth uncharacteristic for a theoretical physicist.

---

## 6.7 Self-Management and Discipline Assets

**Teetotalism.** Lifelong, near-absolute, in conscious opposition to the paternal model. This is not merely abstention but a structural commitment that has held under every imaginable stressor.

**Dietary discipline.** Vegetarian for long stretches of the canon; minimalist; ascetic. The subject does not use food for comfort, which in a complex-trauma profile is unusual and prognostically favorable.

**Sleep and arousal monitoring.** The subject has, across decades, developed sophisticated somatic literacy regarding his own autonomic state — pulse, respiration, muscle tone, the prodromal signs of dissociative switch. He can buy himself minutes that no untrained operator could. He carries (in various eras) a pulse monitor as habit, not affectation.

**Meditation and breath practice.** Sustained engagement with pranayama, zazen, and tantric techniques during his Tibetan and South Asian periods. These have measurable effect on transformation threshold.

**Anchor objects and rituals.** Carries — across continuities — a small photograph of his mother; sometimes a wedding band; a worn book. The reliance on portable, sentimental anchors is the deliberate self-treatment of a man who knows he will lose every fixed thing.

---

## 6.8 Resilience Factors (Structural)

**Survival drive that operates below the suicidal layer.** The subject has attempted suicide; the *body* has refused. But beneath the suicidality there is also, in the host, a quiet refusal to quit — visible in the doggedness with which he returns to therapy, returns to Betty, returns to the work, returns to the world after each exile. The depression is real; the will underneath it is also real.

**Meaning-making capacity.** The subject reliably constructs frameworks of meaning around his condition — duty, service, atonement, science — that allow him to continue functioning. Frankl's observation that those who have a *why* can bear almost any *how* is a fair description of this case.

**Humor.** Sparse, dry, self-deprecating, and present. The host can make a joke at his own expense without bitterness. This is a higher-order defense and an indicator of intact ego function beneath the wound.

**Curiosity.** Has never fully extinguished, even in the worst periods. The subject in flight phases still reads, still studies, still attends to phenomena. Curiosity is the rope that connects the adult to the parts of childhood that were not destroyed.

**Capacity to receive help, intermittently.** Not consistent, but present — from Samson, from Betty, from Strange, from the Warbound. The capacity exists; it requires the right relational conditions.

**Pattern recognition about his own pattern.** The subject knows the cycle (stressor → suppression → arousal → breach → flight → tighter containment). The knowledge does not yet break the cycle, but knowing the cycle is the precondition for breaking it.

---

## 6.9 The Convertible Assets — Liability Faces of Strength

Several items belong on both ledgers and are most accurately recorded here as **assets pending the right intervention**:

- **Hyper-vigilance** — disabling at baseline; in tactical and diagnostic contexts, the same capacity produces threat assessment of unusual quality.
- **Isolation tolerance** — pathological in attachment terms; operationally, it permits long covert deployments no other operator could sustain.
- **Reaction-formation gentleness** — defensive in origin; functionally produces a clinician's bedside manner and a teacher's patience.
- **The introjected paternal voice (Devil Hulk)** — a persecutor for decades; latterly demonstrated reconfigurable as protector. The introject is the case's worst object and, paradoxically, its most powerful one.
- **The somatic literalization of dissociation** — the central tragedy of the case; also the source of the planetary-tier capability that has saved more lives than any other single asset in the file.

---

## 6.10 Summary Judgment

The subject is, on the asset side, **a high-capability operator with intact conscience, exceptional cognition, planetary-tier somatic capability, a durable if narrow attachment base, a covertly cooperative internal system, and the rare reflective capacity to know what is wrong with him.** The pathology is severe and the file's earlier sections do not understate it. But the resilience inventory is, by any honest reading, equally severe in the other direction. He has been treated rarely and protected less; what he has accomplished, he has accomplished from inside the wound, mostly alone. A case file that did not record this would not be intelligence — it would be prosecution.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION — SUBJECT: BANNER, R.B.

*A longitudinal map of how this subject breaks. Read alongside §3 (Psychological) and §4 (Psychiatric). The collapse architecture in this case is unusually well-documented because every decompensation event is also a public event: the subject cannot fail privately. Sixty years of recorded breaches give us an unusually high-resolution map of the staging, somatic markers, environmental triggers, and post-event sequelae.*

---

## 1. THE BASELINE FROM WHICH HE BREAKS

To understand the decompensation pattern, the baseline must first be characterized precisely, because the subject's "stable" state is itself a heavily engineered, high-effort performance — not a true resting state. What an external observer would record as "Banner functioning normally" is in fact a continuous act of suppression, requiring:

- **Continuous cardiac self-monitoring.** Across the canon the subject is depicted touching his wrist, his carotid, his chest; checking his pulse against a watch face; pausing mid-sentence to re-regulate breath. Late-period observers (Ewing) explicitly note he sleeps with a heart-rate monitor and wakes when it alarms. This is not a quirk; it is the subject treating his autonomic nervous system as a hostile external system requiring telemetry.
- **Caloric and stimulant restriction.** Subject avoids caffeine, refuses alcohol entirely (see §2 — the not-his-father organization), eats sparingly, and is repeatedly depicted with under-eaten food in front of him. The body is kept lean and low-arousal as a chronic suppression strategy.
- **Environmental pre-clearance.** In any new room the subject's gaze scans for exits, breakables, civilian density, and structural integrity. This is recorded as early as the Trimpe-era flight sequences and is consistent through Aaron and Ewing.
- **Speech compression.** In stable state, sentences are short, voice is low-volume, pronouns ("I") are softened or omitted. He uses passive constructions where assertion would be appropriate ("it might be possible to…" rather than "I will…"). This is the linguistic signature of a host who experiences self-assertion as dangerous.
- **Physical compression.** Shoulders forward, arms close to torso, often hands in pockets or clasped — making himself small. Bruce Timm and successive artists have rendered this consistently across half a century.

The baseline, then, is **a continuous low-grade hypervigilant performance** that consumes most of the subject's executive resources. This matters because decompensation is not the failure of an ordinary equilibrium; it is the failure of a difficult one. The subject is always already close to the edge. What looks like a sudden break is the collapse of an unsustainable scaffold.

---

## 2. THE ESCALATION PATH — STAGED

The escalation has been documented enough times that it can be parsed into discrete, observable stages. The transitions between stages are not always linear; the subject can spend hours at Stage II or skip directly from I to V given the right stimulus. The map below describes the *modal* path.

### Stage I — Stressor Onset / Cognitive Capture

A trigger appears in the environment. The subject's first response is **cognitive**: he attempts to construct an explanatory frame, often verbalized ("Okay — okay, let me think. Let me think about this."). Speech rate may briefly *increase* as intellectualization is recruited. Eye contact is maintained but flattens. The subject may sit down, ostensibly to reason, actually to lower postural arousal.

*Observable markers:* increased blink rate; subject removes glasses to polish them (recurrent across decades — a self-soothing micro-ritual recoded as analytical pause); subject begins a sentence about probabilities or thresholds; subject excuses himself to "step outside."

### Stage II — Containment Recruitment

The subject begins to deploy explicit regulation: breath control (counted inhalations, often four-in-six-out), pulse check, sometimes a half-spoken mantra ("calm, calm, I'm calm," or in later eras the explicit therapeutic phrases drilled with Samson). He will physically separate himself from the stressor — walks to a window, leaves the room, asks the others to back away. This is the most prosocial stage and the one in which observers often misread him as in control.

*Observable markers:* the subject's hands begin to tremble at fine-motor scale (visible in pen-holding, glasses-handling); sweat at temples and upper lip; a specific tell of the lower jaw setting and re-setting; perseverative apologies ("I'm sorry, I just — I need a moment"); progressive loss of contractions in speech as cognitive load mounts ("I am sorry. I need to leave now.").

### Stage III — Autonomic Surge

Containment fails to bring pulse down. Pulse climbs through the subject's known threshold zone (varies by era but is repeatedly characterized as a sharp transition above the high-100s into a region where suppression becomes impossible). The subject is now aware of imminent loss of control and his communication shifts from prosocial regulation to **warning behavior**: "Get back. Get away from me. Get out." Pronouns disinhibit and become imperative.

*Observable markers:* skin flushes — first across the cheekbones and forehead, then spreading downward and outward; pupils dilate; subject's voice drops in pitch as laryngeal musculature engages; a low groan or grunt — the first non-verbal vocalization, diagnostically critical because the host does not normally vocalize involuntarily; sweating becomes visible across torso; jaw clenches and does not release. The first **chromatic shift** at the periphery — fingertips, eye sclera tinting — has been depicted as occurring in this stage when the breach is imminent.

### Stage IV — Dissociative Switch

The point of executive transfer. The subject's eyes, in nearly every careful artist's rendering of this stage across sixty years, **close briefly and reopen changed** — not because the iris color has yet changed but because the *gaze* has changed: it goes from organized to unorganized, from socially attuned to environmentally scanning, from inhibited to disinhibited. This is the moment of host departure. Audibly the subject often produces a strangled "no" or simply the inhalation that becomes the first roar.

*Observable markers:* the chromatic and morphological transformation, which is the somatic literalization of the switch — but the diagnostically important moment is the **half-second of stillness** that immediately precedes it, the dissociative-fugue onset that observers who know the subject (Betty, Samson, Rick Jones) have learned to recognize as the last window for intervention.

### Stage V — Alter in Field

Executive control is held by whichever alter the environmental cues have summoned. Which alter emerges is not random and is the most overlooked feature of the decompensation pattern. Triggers map to alters:

- **Threat to a child, or to Banner-as-child (restraint, helplessness, being attacked while incapacitated)** → Savage alter. Cognition collapses to ~7-year-old level. Vocabulary regresses to monosyllables and third-person self-reference. Affect is undifferentiated rage and grief.
- **Sustained low-grade humiliation, betrayal, sexual or appetitive frustration, urban/social environments** → the Grey alter. Cognition is preserved; affect is sardonic, predatory, manipulative; the alter often *avoids* combat in favor of social maneuver. Almost exclusively nocturnal.
- **Coordinated, comprehensible threat with a clear narrative justification (war, defense of a defined group, sustained adversarial campaigns)** → the integrated/"Worldbreaker" presentation, where cognition and somatics are both online. The most lethal mode because suppression has been replaced by organization.
- **Internal stressors — recovered memory, self-loathing spirals, dream incursions** → Devil/Guilt alter. This alter rarely takes the field in waking life but is the dominant figure in the subject's hypnagogic and dream landscape and the voice that critiques and degrades the host between episodes.

### Stage VI — Cessation and Re-Entry

The alter's tenure ends when the somatic/autonomic substrate exhausts, when the threat is neutralized, or — rarely — when an external attachment voice (Betty, occasionally Rick) successfully reaches through. Re-entry is consistently traumatic: the host returns to a body in an unfamiliar location, frequently nude (the subject's clothes do not survive transformation; the canonical purple trouser remnant is a long-running gallows joke that is, clinically, a marker of repeated post-fugue exposure), often bloodied, often surrounded by destruction whose meaning he must reconstruct from physical evidence.

*Observable markers:* the host curls into a fetal posture within minutes of re-entry; covers genitals and face; speech returns slowly, monosyllabic at first; first coherent utterances are almost always self-referential and shame-saturated ("Oh god. Oh god, what did I do. Who did I hurt."); subject vomits in roughly a third of recorded re-entries; he will refuse food and water for hours.

### Stage VII — Shame Spiral and Flight

The post-episode period is the second decompensation, layered on the first, and it is the period in which the subject does the most lasting damage to his own treatment trajectory. The host re-establishes containment more rigidly than before, withdraws from any attachment that witnessed the episode (this is the mechanism by which he serially leaves Betty), and embarks on geographic flight — train, road, foreign country, in late eras off-planet. Flight is rationalized as protective of others and is, at the explicit content level, true; at the structural level it is the abused child running.

---

## 3. THE CONDITIONS THAT PRODUCE COLLAPSE

The escalation path describes the mechanism; the conditions describe what trips it. From sixty years of record, the precipitants cluster into recognizable families.

**Acute physical threat to attachment figures.** The fastest and most complete decompensations in the file are produced by threat to Betty Ross. The subject loses Stage II entirely and proceeds I → III → IV in seconds. Threat to Rick Jones has produced similar acceleration. Threat to himself produces, paradoxically, a slower curve — the subject's self-preservation drive is weak; his other-preservation drive is the central organizing affect.

**Children in danger.** Touches the unprotected-child substrate directly. Produces specifically Savage alter emergence even where the environmental sophistication would predict a different presentation. The subject cannot witness child endangerment without breaching.

**Restraint and confinement.** Among the highest-magnitude triggers in the file. Cuffs, cells, sedation against will, surgical restraint, military containment apparatus — these reproduce the somatic helplessness of the abused child and produce the most violent alter responses on record. Any therapeutic or institutional setting that uses restraint is contraindicated and has, in practice, produced catastrophic incidents.

**Paternal-coded authority deploying contempt.** General Ross is the recurring precipitant here, but the pattern generalizes to any older male in a position of power who addresses the subject with derogation. The host regresses and submits — and the alter, hours or days later, retaliates. The latency is diagnostically important: the host swallows the contempt; the alter remembers.

**Forced recollection.** Therapeutic, pharmacological, or hostile attempts to surface the childhood material before the subject's defenses are ready to hold it. Produces the largest single decompensations in the record (the Samson sessions of the late 1980s, the Ewing-era memory recoveries). Conversely, *unforced* recollection within a trusted alliance has produced the only durable gains.

**Being named monster.** A specific verbal stimulus. The word "monster" or its semantic equivalents collapses any therapeutic gain in progress. This is because the subject's self-concept and the Devil-alter's introjected voice both use that exact word; external use confirms and amplifies the internal one.

**Sleep deprivation.** The subject's nocturnal vulnerability is documented from the Lee/Kirby era forward. The original transformations were nocturnal; the Grey alter is nocturnal; the dream incursions of the Devil alter are nocturnal. Disrupted sleep — common in his transient lifestyle — lowers the threshold for breach across all alter pathways.

**Disinhibitor exposure.** Although the subject is teetotal, involuntary exposure (drugged drink, gas attack, neuro-chemical manipulation) bypasses the host's suppression scaffolding entirely and produces immediate Stage III–IV transitions. Adversaries who have understood this have exploited it; the SHIELD and AIM files on the subject reflect this knowledge.

**Pain.** Acute physical pain, especially gunshot, blade, or burn, has near-zero latency to transformation. The subject's body has learned that pain means a child being struck; the dissociative response is essentially reflexive.

**Sustained social proximity at moderate-intensity intimacy.** Worth naming separately because it is the most insidious condition: not crisis but ordinary closeness held over time. Living with Betty for weeks. Working with a team for months. The cumulative autonomic load of being *seen* exceeds the host's window of tolerance more reliably than any acute stressor, which is the structural reason the subject cannot stay anywhere.

---

## 4. WHAT THE COLLAPSE LOOKS LIKE — TYPOLOGY

Decompensations in the record fall into recognizable types. Naming them matters because the intervention pathway differs by type.

**Type A — Acute reactive.** Trigger is external and time-limited (attack, accident, attempted murder of a bystander). Escalation is fast (seconds), Savage alter typically emerges, destruction is local, cessation is achieved when the threat ends or the alter's metabolic substrate exhausts. Re-entry is acute but the host's narrative reconstruction is comparatively coherent ("they attacked us — I changed — people are hurt"). Frequency: most common type in the file.

**Type B — Cumulative.** Trigger is the slow accretion of social or affective load over hours or days. Escalation has long Stage I and II, with the host visibly trying and failing; the breach when it comes is often in privacy (motel room, lab) and the alter that emerges is more often Grey than Savage. Destruction is diffuse and the alter may absent itself for days. Re-entry is dispersed in time and the host may reconstruct the gap only with difficulty. This is the type that drives the serial-flight pattern.

**Type C — Anniversary / commemorative.** Surrounding the subject's mother's death date and around significant relational anniversaries with Betty, the subject's threshold drops measurably without an identifiable acute trigger. Episodes during these periods are over-determined and disproportionately involve the Devil alter at the dream/intrusion level.

**Type D — Iatrogenic.** Produced by treatment, restraint, weaponization, or research intervention. Among the worst decompensations on record (the gamma-cell sequences, the various containment-facility incidents). The presence of paternal-coded authority and restraint in combination essentially guarantees a maximum-magnitude event.

**Type E — Suicidal contraction.** The least-visible decompensation: the subject does not transform but instead enters a state of acute hopelessness, plans and sometimes attempts self-destruction by means designed to bypass the alter's protection (the "Hulk-proof bullet" attempt). The body intercepts; the host wakes intact and more demoralized, which feeds the next cycle.

**Type F — Integrative breakdown.** Rare and significant. Occurs during genuine therapeutic progress when defensive structures loosen faster than integrative capacity grows. The host experiences identity diffusion, multiple alters surface simultaneously or in rapid sequence, and the Devil alter speaks audibly. These episodes look like catastrophe from outside but are, in trauma-therapy terms, the painful work of dismantling the dissociative apparatus. The *Immortal Hulk*–era breakdowns belong to this type and represent the only decompensations in the record with prognostic upside.

---

## 5. THE INTER-EPISODE PERIOD — WHERE THE REAL PATHOLOGY LIVES

Surveillance attention concentrates on the transformations because they are spectacular. The clinical reality is that the most pathological time in the subject's life is the period *between* episodes, because it is during this period that the structures producing the next episode are reinforced.

In the inter-episode period the subject:

- Reviews the prior episode in solitary, obsessive replay (the canon shows him watching news footage, reading reports, examining his own wounds in mirrors). This is not integration; it is rumination feeding the Devil alter.
- Tightens his containment regime — adds new monitoring protocols, restricts diet further, isolates more aggressively, refuses overtures of contact.
- Composes and then does not send messages to Betty. The drafts-folder-of-the-life pattern is documented across decades.
- Conducts physics work at high intensity — productive output is highest in the immediate post-episode period because intellectualization is most heavily recruited then.
- Experiences progressively worse sleep, more vivid dream incursions of the Devil alter, and a measurable shortening of the latency to next breach.

The inter-episode period, in other words, is not recovery. It is the staging ground for the next decompensation. The subject's recurring tragedy is that he has spent most of his adult life mistaking the staging ground for safety.

---

## 6. WHAT INTERVENES — WHAT REACHES THROUGH

For completeness, and because the absence of these conditions is itself part of the decompensation profile, the file records what has, on rare occasions, interrupted the cycle:

- **A specific attachment voice in Stage III or early IV.** Betty's voice, calling the subject by his given name in a register that is neither command nor fear, has aborted transitions on multiple occasions. Rick Jones's voice has on rare occasions done the same. No other voice is reliably effective.
- **Physical touch from an attachment figure** — hand to face, forehead to forehead — in early Stage IV. This is the somatic counterpart of the verbal intervention and works through the same attachment substrate.
- **The subject's own articulated permission to feel the affect** — i.e., the host saying, in the late Ewing-era language, some version of *"it's allowed to be here"* — which has, when achievable, prevented breach by removing the suppression that is itself the destabilizer.
- **A coherent ally-alter relationship** rather than host-vs-alter opposition. The integrative work of the late period shows that when the host stops trying to suppress and instead negotiates with the alter system, breaches decrease in frequency and severity.

The throughline is that what intervenes is **relational and integrative**, never restrictive. Every restrictive intervention in the file has made the next decompensation worse. This is the central operational conclusion of the failure-modes analysis: the subject does not break because of insufficient containment. He breaks because containment is the mechanism of breaking. The dissociative apparatus is the wound; the wound is reopened every time the host treats his own affect as something to be locked away rather than known.

He has rarely been offered the alternative. When he has, he has used it. That is the prognostic note that closes this section, and it is consistent with the etiological conclusion of §4: the subject is treatable. The conditions of his life have, with rare exceptions, treated him as a containment problem rather than a person, and the failure-mode record is the record of what that mistake costs.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT — SUBJECT: BANNER, ROBERT BRUCE, PhD

---

## 6.1 Preamble: The Shape of the Curve

The subject's life arc, plotted across six decades of observation, does not describe a progression toward stable resolution nor a degenerative slide toward terminal collapse. It describes an **asymptotic oscillation around an unreached integration** — a sine wave whose amplitude has, on the longest time-base, slowly decreased while never crossing into flatline. Each major arc resolves with the subject marginally more aware of his own structure and marginally less able to deny it; each subsequent arc reopens the wound at a slightly deeper layer. The trajectory is therefore neither linear improvement nor decline but **spiral**, in the technical trauma-therapy sense: the same material is revisited at progressively deeper strata, and the question for forward assessment is not whether the spiral continues but whether it tightens toward a center (integration) or loosens toward dispersal (system collapse).

What follows is the file's projection of where that spiral is headed, the discrete fork-points at which its direction will be decided, the conditions that would push it toward growth versus catastrophe, and the open empirical questions on which the prognosis depends.

---

## 6.2 The Base-Rate Projection — What Happens If Nothing Changes

If no novel intervention is introduced and the subject is left to his established coping repertoire — flight, intellectualization, instrumentalization of the alter system, intermittent and partial therapeutic contact — the base-rate projection is **continuation of the cycle at decreasing intervals**. The pattern across the file is that the latency between dissociative breaches has shortened over the subject's lifetime as the somatic substrate has become more practiced at switching and as the host's containment regime, however rigorous, has become progressively less novel and therefore less effective. The subject's body has learned the pathway. The pathway gets faster each time it is run.

Under this projection, expect: (a) further geographic flight episodes at intervals correlated with the depth of any attempted intimacy; (b) periodic suicidal ideation and one or more attempts, all somatically interdicted by the regenerative state, each such interdiction constituting an additional iatrogenic trauma layered on the existing structure; (c) further emergence of previously sequestered alter material as the dissociative architecture under chronic load develops new compartments to hold what the existing ones cannot; (d) periodic apparent integrations followed by destabilization, with the Devil Hulk introject reasserting precedence under sufficient stress; (e) ongoing oscillation between Avengers-affiliated periods and total withdrawal periods, the affiliation periods serving as functional containment while not addressing the wound.

The base-rate endpoint is not death — the regenerative substrate has effectively foreclosed that exit — but **chronic suspended decompensation**: a state in which the subject is unable to die, unable to integrate, and unable to sustain any environment in which integration could occur. This is the prognosis the file regards as most probable under inertia.

---

## 6.3 The Two Attractors

Around this base-rate trajectory orbit two attractor states, either of which could absorb the system if conditions tip far enough.

### 6.3.1 The Growth Attractor — Cooperative Multiplicity

The model the file regards as the correct clinical direction, foreshadowed in the late canon, is **functional cooperative multiplicity** — not "cure" in the sense of fusion to a single identity, but a negotiated internal federation in which each alter retains its function, its memory, and its voice, and in which the host is one member of a council rather than a denying executive. Contemporary trauma practice has largely abandoned forced integration in favor of this model precisely because forced integration tends to produce structural rebound (the suppressed alter returns more virulently). The subject's case is unusually well-suited to this approach because his alters are highly differentiated, articulate, and — in the Professor and even, intermittently, the Savage state — capable of recognizing the others' legitimacy.

Under this attractor: the Savage Hulk is recognized as the seven-year-old child holding the matricide and is treated accordingly (not suppressed, not deployed, but *protected*); the Grey/Fixit alter is recognized as the carrier of disinhibited drive and given limited, negotiated executive time in low-risk contexts; the Professor state is recognized as a coalition rather than a sovereign; and the Devil Hulk — the hardest piece — is reframed from persecutor to **misidentified protector**: the introjected father's voice retained because, in the child's logic, identification with the aggressor was the only available survival strategy, and the alter therefore functions, perversely, as a guard against re-victimization. Reframing the Devil Hulk as a damaged ally rather than an enemy to be exiled is the single most consequential therapeutic move available to the subject, and the late canon has begun to gesture toward it.

The somatic question — what happens to the body under cooperative multiplicity — is the case's true open problem. The provisional answer suggested by the trajectory is that as inter-alter conflict decreases, the somatic violence of switching decreases proportionally; the transformation becomes less catastrophic, less involuntary, more graduated. The endpoint of this attractor is not a man who never transforms but a man whose transformation is no longer a rupture.

### 6.3.2 The Catastrophe Attractor — The Devil Hulk Ascendant

The opposing attractor, equally consistent with the structure, is **persecutor-alter takeover**. Under sustained stress without therapeutic support, the internal hierarchy can invert: the Devil Hulk introject, which speaks in the father's register and wishes the host destroyed, can become the dominant executive. The mechanism is not mysterious — it is the standard structural-dissociation outcome when the host's coping capacity is exhausted and a more aggressive alter offers the only available path through.

The catastrophe under this attractor is not simple destructiveness. The Savage Hulk has been destructive for sixty years and the world has survived it. The catastrophe specific to Devil Hulk ascendancy is **organized, intelligent, sustained malevolence directed by the introjected abuser through the somatic substrate of the most physically formidable being in the canon**. This is the worst-case scenario the file recognizes and it is not speculative; the late canon has explicitly staged it. The conditions that would precipitate it are catalogued in §6.5 below.

---

## 6.4 Likely Future Developments — Specific Predictions

Working from the established patterns, the following developments are projected with the indicated confidence:

**High confidence (>80%).**
- Further cycles of Betty-pursuit / Betty-withdrawal, with each cycle producing partial insight followed by partial regression. The Betty relationship is the subject's only sustained attachment and will therefore continue to function as both the chief therapeutic resource and the chief decompensating trigger.
- Continued emergence of previously unmapped alters or alter-fragments as the dissociative architecture continues to differentiate under load. Expect at minimum one additional childhood-age fragment and, possibly, a maternal-introject alter (the mother has been almost entirely absent from the alter system, which is itself diagnostically suggestive — the mother-introject may have been too painful to constellate and may yet emerge).
- Periodic attempts at instrumentalization (military, governmental, team-affiliated) that the subject will rationalize as containment-via-utility and that will fail on the same grounds previous attempts have failed: they address deployment rather than wound.
- Further suicidality, somatically foreclosed, producing additional iatrogenic trauma. This is the file's most distressing high-confidence prediction.

**Moderate confidence (40–70%).**
- A discrete recovered-memory event involving previously sequestered material — most plausibly involving the mother, the matricide itself in more granular detail, or some element of the father's behavior not yet on the record. Such events have historically produced the largest single decompensations in the file and the next one will likely be larger.
- A period of relative stabilization lasting on the order of years, mediated by a sustained therapeutic alliance (Samson, or a successor), terminated by an external destabilizer rather than by internal failure.
- Re-emergence of the Devil Hulk in dialogue rather than suppression — the necessary precondition for the growth attractor.

**Low confidence but high consequence (10–30%).**
- Devil Hulk ascendancy as described in §6.3.2.
- Permanent loss of host executive function via prolonged dissociative fugue from which the host does not resurface, with the alter system continuing to operate the body indefinitely. The subject's body's apparent immortality makes this scenario, uniquely in the file, a *longer* projection than the subject's biological lifespan would otherwise allow.
- Genuine cooperative multiplicity achieved and sustained for more than five subjective years — the growth attractor reached and held. This is rated low-confidence not because it is implausible in principle but because the environmental conditions for it have never assembled in the subject's life and there is no obvious mechanism by which they would.

---

## 6.5 Fork Points — The Specific Conditions That Will Decide Direction

The trajectory is not continuous; it pivots at identifiable junctures. The file flags the following as the discrete fork-points whose resolution will determine which attractor the system enters.

**Fork 1: The Next Major Loss.** The subject has not yet, in the canon's accounting, lost Betty permanently in a way he cannot rationalize as temporary. The death or unequivocal departure of Betty Ross is the single largest pending stressor on the system. Under growth conditions (concurrent therapeutic alliance, alter cooperation, safe environment) the subject could metabolize this loss as the first adult grief he has been permitted to experience consciously and the experience could itself be integrative. Under catastrophe conditions (isolated, no alliance, Devil Hulk active) the same loss is the most probable single precipitant of persecutor-alter takeover. The fork is the same event; the determinant is the surrounding scaffold.

**Fork 2: The Next Containment Attempt by Paternal Authority.** General Ross or a successor figure will, at intervals, attempt forcible containment. Each such attempt re-stages the original power asymmetry. Whether the subject responds with regression-and-rage (the established pattern) or with negotiated refusal-from-strength depends on whether by that point the Devil Hulk introject has been reframed as ally or remains as persecutor — because the subject cannot stand up to an external father while an internal father is still telling him he deserves destruction.

**Fork 3: The Next Recovered Memory.** As above; the event is coming, the question is the scaffold present when it arrives.

**Fork 4: The Subject's Decision Regarding Children.** This is the file's least-discussed but most diagnostically loaded fork. The subject has consistently and explicitly refused fatherhood on the grounds that he is genetically and behaviorally too dangerous to reproduce. This refusal is overdetermined: it reflects realistic risk assessment, but it also reflects exact identification with his father's paranoid belief about *his* genetic contamination of *him* — i.e., the subject has internalized the father's stated rationale for the abuse as his own rationale for self-foreclosure. If the subject can in future distinguish his own moral judgment about reproduction from his father's introjected voice about contamination — regardless of which decision he then reaches — that distinction is itself diagnostic of integration. If he cannot, the foreclosure remains a continuous low-grade confirmation that the father was right.

**Fork 5: The Therapeutic Successor Question.** Samson is the subject's only sustained therapeutic relationship and Samson is not permanent. The presence or absence of a successor at the moment Samson is removed from the picture is a binary fork. There is no functional substitute in the subject's existing network.

---

## 6.6 What Would Push Toward Growth — Specific Mechanisms

Growth in this case is not mysterious and does not require novel theory. It requires the following, all of which are knowable and most of which have at various points been partially present:

1. **A sustained safe relational environment over a multi-year timescale.** The subject has never had this in adulthood. The longest stable period in the file is on the order of months. Multi-year stability would itself be therapeutic by base rate, independent of any specific intervention.

2. **Continued inter-alter dialogue rather than suppression.** The late canon's movement in this direction must be sustained and elaborated. Specifically: the Devil Hulk must be addressed *in dialogue*, not exiled, not killed (attempts to kill internal alters in trauma work reliably produce structural rebound), but slowly reframed from persecutor to traumatized-protector.

3. **A reparative paternal figure in the subject's life.** The subject has never had a non-abusive sustained male attachment that occupied the paternal role. Samson is professional; Stark is peer; Rogers is briefly approximate but never sustained. A genuine reparative paternal relationship — slow, undemanding, reliable — would do work no other intervention can do, because it would offer the introjected father a competitor in the internal landscape.

4. **Permission to feel anger at the host level in safe contexts.** The subject's defining incapacity is the host's complete interdiction of anger. Graduated, low-stakes practice with conscious anger in safe relational contexts is the standard trauma-therapy approach and would reduce the load on the dissociative apparatus. The subject has, to the file's knowledge, never been offered or accepted this practice.

5. **Mourning the mother.** The mother is the case's missing piece. The matricide has been recovered as memory but never adequately grieved as loss. Conscious mourning of Rebecca Banner, with the affect she is owed, is a required station of integration that has not yet been reached.

6. **Conscious mourning of the father.** Harder, but necessary. The subject must at some point mourn not the father he had but the father he should have had and did not — and, separately, mourn the father he had as a damaged human being rather than only fear him as a monster. This is the move that disarms the Devil Hulk introject, because it relocates the father from internal persecutor to external tragedy.

---

## 6.7 What Would Push Toward Catastrophe

Symmetrically:

1. **Sustained isolation without therapeutic contact**, especially in conjunction with chronic external threat — the precise conditions under which the persecutor alter has historically gained ground.
